Rogers

Within the Week Departing from America to China 36

U.S. Senate Asks for Treasury Secretary

To Prove Silver Hoarding Allegations

(Washington) Today, the Senate passed Senator Robinson's bill, which requests Treasury Secretary Morgenthau to provide a list of silver hoarders, as the Treasury Secretary had previously indicated that silver proponents intended to exploit the silver issue to purchase silver. Furthermore, according to sources close to the White House, the government has decided to adopt a delaying policy regarding this session's silver bill. Professor Rogers, a presidential advisor and renowned economist from Yale University, will depart from America for China within this week to represent the government in studying the impact of American silver policy on China and Sino-American trade issues. According to Senator Wheeler, a leader of the silver faction, Professor Rogers' return to the U.S. is expected to be around July 4th at the earliest, rendering it ineffective for this session of Congress. The Senate Agriculture Committee today approved Punkhearst's cotton restriction bill. According to Punkhearst himself, the bill is expected to pass the Senate soon. The bill has been subject to intense debate for a long time, as Republican senators have consistently opposed it, arguing that the forced restriction of cotton production is the first step towards agricultural collectivization. Republican representatives in the House also hold this view, even though the bill has already been safely passed in the House. For example, last year, Japan's exports of cotton fabrics were greater than those of Lancashire, which is the only time this has ever happened in history." (Havas Telegram of the 21st)

Page 8

Roosevelt Takes on a Difficult Task

Efforts to Mediate Capital Disputes 40

Warns Auto Industry to Stop Fighting

Union Announces Postponement of General Strike

First Test of Labor Regulations

(Washington) President Roosevelt, during this tense situation, once again took on a difficult task as he did during last year's banking panic, seeking the public's welfare and maintaining peace in the business world. The auto industry labor unrest will not develop before the owners convene in White Sulphur Springs. Attendees are expected to include Chrysler, Sloan, and Axel Ford, all giants in the auto industry. The New York correspondence from Washington expects that if manufacturers insist on not recognizing the union's right to collective bargaining, the government will express its labor policy. Today, the President may discuss the matter of the auto industry being licensed to comply with the National Recovery Administration's work regulations. At the same time, the government has now requested the Delaware court to enjoin Weiton Iron Company from violating steel industry regulations. This action by the government is the first legal test of the effectiveness of the Recovery Administration's labor regulations. The dispute between the company and the National Labor Relations Board has now reached its peak. (Reuters Telegram of the 21st)

(Washington) In the midst of a highly tense strike situation, the courageous President Roosevelt issued a serious warning today to representatives of both the union and capital, stating that the President will take decisive action to prevent conflicts between labor and capital in order to protect the public interest. (National Telegram of the 20th)

The labor dispute in the American auto industry in Michigan announced a truce today due to President Roosevelt's intervention. Auto industry worker leaders, in order to comply with President Roosevelt's proposal, have agreed to postpone tomorrow's strike in order to await the outcome of the White House roundtable meeting on Thursday. The meeting to be held at the White House on Thursday will be attended by auto industry owners, union leaders, government officials, and other key figures related to the strike. Since President Roosevelt's timely halt and the Detroit worker leaders' decision were spread, the entire area today was filled with joy, because merchants and citizens alike believed that a general strike by auto industry workers would increase social conflict. (National Telegram of the 20th)

(Washington) If the final efforts to mediate the labor dispute fail, America will face its largest strike in history tomorrow. The American Federation of Labor (AFL) claims that 100,000 auto industry workers are prepared to begin striking at 9:00 a.m. tomorrow. President Roosevelt has telegraphed the AFL, urging them to postpone the strike action for one day. The AFL's reply telegram can be sent tonight. Auto industry owners are now, on the advice of National Recovery Administration Director Johnson, sending representatives to Washington to meet with the President on Wednesday. AFL President Green telegraphed Collins, the AFL representative in New York, today, urging him to comply with the President's wishes and postpone the strike, at least until Thursday. Collins then telegraphed the President, saying that AFL officers are scheduled to meet in Pontiac, Michigan, at 5:00 p.m. tonight to discuss this matter. At that time, he will advise them to follow the authorities' intentions and deal with everything in a peaceful spirit. A certain auto parts factory in Detroit has already started striking, and 16,000 workers at the Chevrolet plant in Flint, Michigan, have voted to strike. However, better news has come out of Pontiac tonight, saying that auto industry union leaders have agreed to a truce. Railway managers are demanding a 15% wage cut starting July 1st, while railway employees are demanding a 20% wage increase from the same date. The President warned both sides to resolve it peacefully, or he would appoint a public committee to study the dispute. The President advocated extending the current 10% wage cut for six months, while also notifying the Railway Bureau that he felt that some wages, even if not lower than the cost of living, were not as low as the minimum wage set by the Recovery Administration. Today, the Railway Bureau managers have agreed to accept the President's proposal to extend the existing wage rate to December 31st. The President is scheduled to meet today to make a final effort to reconcile the labor dispute and avoid tomorrow's strike. (Reuters Telegram of the 20th)

(Washington) After President Roosevelt mediated the auto industry dispute, a question has now been raised: will the American auto industry, which employs 250,000 workers and produces three-quarters of the world's total output of automobiles, be subject to government control? President Roosevelt, based on the National Industrial Recovery Act, can use his power to force auto factories to obtain government licenses. Those who do not comply with the regulations set by the President will not be able to obtain them. What the future holds will depend on the outcome of tomorrow's meeting between President Roosevelt and the auto factory committee. (Reuters Telegram of the 21st)

A Bomb!

Göring Narrowly Escapes Danger 41

Accidentally Hits Streetcar Driver

(Berlin) Today, someone attempted to assassinate Prussian Prime Minister General Göring and National Socialist Party leader Ernst. When the two were driving past the Prussian administrative office, a bomb was suddenly thrown from a building under repair. However, because the aim was inaccurate, it only hit a passing streetcar, injuring the driver. The police are currently investigating the matter. (Reuters Telegram of the 21st)

Czech Foreign Minister Expresses

A Solution for the Austrian Question 42

European Countries Participate in Economic Cooperation Together

Czech Republic Ready to Negotiate Commercial Treaty with Hungary

Prague Czech Foreign Minister Beneš delivered a speech to the Foreign Affairs Committee of the Lower House this morning regarding the Austrian question. He first stated that there are four solutions to the Austrian question: First, the annexation of Austria by Germany to solve the Austrian question. This solution cannot be accepted due to the restrictions of international treaties. Second, the solution proposed by Italy of a tripartite alliance between Italy, Austria, and Hungary to prevent the annexation of Austria by Germany. This is unacceptable to the Little Entente countries because it contradicts the protocols of 1922 and 1932 regarding the Austrian question. Third, the Central European solution, which is to organize the Danube League or the Austro-Hungarian Confederation to solve the Austrian question. However, the Danube League may pose a danger of restoring the old Habsburg Empire, while the Austro-Hungarian Confederation would inevitably divide the Danube countries into two major groups, opposing each other, which would be enough to bury the seeds of lasting conflict, and would also be a preparation for the resurgence of the Habsburg dynasty. This is even more unacceptable to the Little Entente countries. Since the above three solutions cannot solve the Austrian question, the only viable solution is the fourth, the European solution. The so-called European solution is that European countries that signed the 1922 protocol jointly guarantee Austria's absolute independence, and that Austria obtains certain economic benefits based on the discussions of the Stresa Danube Economic Conference and Mussolini's memorandum. In other words, no country should be excluded from this kind of economic cooperation. Finally, Beneš declared that the Czech government is prepared to participate in various discussions so that it can reopen commercial negotiations with Hungary in the near future. (Havas Telegram of the 21st)

Hitler's Four-Year Plan

Construction Relieves Unemployment 43

New Car Road to Austria Border

Allow 300,000 Women to Marry Annually

(Berlin) The four-year movement to improve work initiated by German Chancellor Hitler last year has reduced the number of unemployed people in Germany by one-third in the past twelve months. The second year of the movement will begin tomorrow. Chancellor Hitler will stand in a car on the newly built car road from Munich to the Austrian border and speak to the workers, and his speech will be broadcast everywhere via radio. Workers across the country will stop work for half an hour to listen quietly to Hitler's speech on the administrative procedures for the coming year. The main points will be large-scale construction projects, such as building car roads and reclaiming wasteland. It is estimated that this procedure will provide year-round employment for two million people. (Reuters Telegram of the 19th)

(Berlin) Today, German Chancellor Hitler and many cabinet members delivered the first of many radio addresses from a car on the road from Munich to the Austrian border to commemorate his seizing of power. He stated that he will allocate 1 billion marks to combat unemployment, and that the government plans to allow 300,000 women to marry this year, and prepare 150 million marks for marriage loans, while allocating 600 million marks to build highways. The government has decided to maintain the stability of the mark's value, and he will absolutely prohibit any attempt to increase prices for dividends. From then on, commerce and industry will not be restricted by legislation. The government will encourage all legitimate businessmen and industrialists, but the government will never subsidize industry again. Propaganda Minister Goebbels also gave a speech, stating that Germany's government's achievement last year of allowing 2.7 million Germans to regain employment has won the praise of those who are arrogant in the world. When the German Chancellor spoke, flags were hung everywhere, and all workers across the country suspended work for one and a half hours to listen quietly. (Reuters Telegram of the 21st)

France Busts Spy Ring

Leader is an American 44

Up to Twenty-Five People Arrested

(Paris) According to official news today, American youth Schwartz of New York has confessed to being the leader of an international spy ring stationed in Paris, specializing in serving the Soviet Union and Germany. The international spy ring has been operating in the United Kingdom, the United States, and France for several years. Its task is to steal military secrets and other news for reference by their employers during wartime. According to police authorities, based on Schwartz's confession, five new criminals have been arrested. The number of members of the group arrested in Paris has now reached twenty-five. Police authorities continued that Schwartz was promoted to leader a year ago. At that time, the former leader of the spy ring was still in Paris, but because the surveillance was tight, he was almost arrested and had to leave France. Professor Retsch of the Paris Institute of Biology is also one of those arrested. It is heard that a great deal of information about the manufacture of French poison gas and secret information about French dignitaries was stolen by Retsch. (National Telegram of the 21st)

(Washington) Today, the U.S. State Department claimed that it had not heard of Schwartz's confession at the Paris police station, but according to Paris police authorities, Schwartz has confessed to being the leader of an international spy ring. It is claimed that the U.S. Ambassador to France has not reported the spy ring incident here, so the State Department will not express anything for the time being. (National Telegram of the 20th)

British Newspaper Advocates

Returning German Territories 45

British Trusteeship of Three African Locations Ineffective

(London) The territories of Togo, Cameroon, and Tanganyika in Africa were German colonies before the war. The Treaty of Versailles stipulated after the war that Germany give up its territorial rights to these territories, and the League of Nations entrusted the United Kingdom to administer them. British newspaper tycoon Lord Rothermere (who recently announced his support for pan-Germanism) recently published an article in the Daily Mail proposing that the British government should return the trusteeship rights of these three locations to the League of Nations so that these three locations can still be used as German territory. The reason is that most of the expenses of these three locations come from subsidies from the British government, while the benefits are obtained by German expatriates. Therefore, it is better to return them to Germany. (Havas Telegram of the 21st)

Soviet New Creation

Amphibious Aircraft 46

Great Progress in Manufacturing Technology

Almost Attempted Suicide Out of Grief Due to Last Summer's Plane Crash

Technician Kalinin Undertakes Second Great Project

(Moscow) The State-owned Civil Aviation Department's Aircraft Scientific Research Institute has manufactured a new [SHI-5] amphibious aircraft. The aircraft was designed by engineer Shavrov and is equipped with two Soviet engines, each with 480 horsepower. It can accommodate fourteen passengers. The aircraft can be used for aerial photography, sowing grains, Arctic expeditions, and ordinary transportation, as well as carrying mail. It can reach an altitude of 6,200 meters, has a speed of 225 kilometers per hour, and can make non-stop flights of 2,000 kilometers. The airframe is mainly made of metal, and the wings are made of wood. It can land on water, ice, and land. (TASS Telegram of the 21st)

(Moscow) It is claimed that Soviet Russia is recently planning to build a huge aircraft to replace the [K-7] aircraft that could carry a hundred people that crashed last summer. It is reported that the aircraft was originally supervised by engineer Kalinin and can be called the largest in the world. When Kalinin heard that the giant aircraft, which was the culmination of his life's efforts, crashed and burned during its test flight, killing fifteen passengers, he was so distraught that he wanted to die. He immediately drafted a suicide note to his family, took a pistol, and went out. It was at this time that Kalinin was summoned to participate in a workers' meeting to mourn those who died in the accident. Kalinin felt grief and sorrow that so many people died due to his technical errors. When he walked into the hall of the memorial service, he learned that something unexpected had happened. The crowd welcomed him warmly. Kalinin was led to the podium and gave a speech to the crowd. Kalinin was so moved that he couldn't say a word for a long time, and tears streamed down his face. The crowd also shed tears of sympathy, mourning the deaths in the accident and regretting the failure of Kalinin's great plan. Kalinin, inspired by the workers' warm sympathy, regained his courage, immediately tore up his farewell letter to his family, abandoned the pistol he was carrying, and resolved to make another effort to build another aircraft, ensuring that there would be no more technical errors. (National Telegram of the 21st)

North is the Yellow River, East is the Grand Canal

(Jinan) Liu Guitang's troops, numbering over a thousand, arrived at Zhongdiquan, 18 miles south of Caoxian on the 17th, where they were met with attacks by the provincial army Wu Yuan and the militia of Gu Liangyou. The cavalry of Yu Tan's reformed troops also pursued from the rear. On the 18th, they fled to Weiji, west of Caoxian, where they were pursued by Wu's militia and ambushed by Gu's militia from Zhuanmiaoji, resulting in the death of over two hundred of Liu's troops. That night, they fled northeast again, passing through Guyingji southwest of Chengwu, to Ranguji and Chenji southeast of Dingtao. On the 19th, they were again ambushed by cavalry and the Dingtao militia. Early this morning, they fled to Taipingji, 65 miles west of Juye, where they were surrounded and attacked by Wu's militia, Gu's militia, and the cavalry of Shi Linqiu's regiment. The battle was fierce, resulting in the death of over two hundred of Liu's troops, the capture of over two hundred, and the killing of over three hundred horses. Over a hundred guns were seized. In the afternoon, they fled to the northwest of Yuncheng. This area is bordered by the Yellow River to the north and the Grand Canal to the east. Liu's troops are trapped. The authorities plan to annihilate Liu's troops there. Ships on both rivers have already been pulled away. Liu's troops are surrounded by water on all sides, and pursued from behind. They have no chance of escape. They now number only six or seven hundred. The authorities expect to resolve the situation in the next day or two. The 22nd Division Commander Gu Liangmin is directing operations in Yuncheng. (21st Dispatch)

(Jinan) Han Tan's and Liu Guitang's troops were intercepted once in Yuncheng last night. Today, they fled to Jinkou, south of Dongping. The remaining bandits number less than a thousand. All are riding donkeys and mules. None are on foot. Because they have been fleeing all day, they are extremely exhausted. There are substantial forces in Dakou, Tai'an, Ningyang, and along the Jinpu Railway. They will definitely not be able to cross and flee back to the mountains of southern Shandong. Those who were on foot have all been killed along the way. The captured Henan cavalry, who pursued to Yuncheng, have been ordered to return to Henan. (21st Dispatch)

Yang Jie's Letter on Italian Military Affairs 58

(Nanjing) Yang Jie recently sent a letter from Germany to a certain military expert, detailing his observations on Italian military affairs. He covered aspects such as the army, navy, air force, party army, aviation industry, armaments industry, automobile industry, and shipbuilding industry. Yang stated that the Italian military is centered on the royal family, with the Fascist Party as its backbone, possessing vigorous spirit and agile operations. The army is divided into thirteen military districts and thirty divisional districts. The navy is divided into four coastal defense districts, each with a commander-in-chief responsible for its area. The air force is divided into three air zones and three auxiliary zones. Specialized schools are established for cultivating military talent. The university party army is a special organization subordinate to the party, responsible for training young party members. The aviation and armaments industries have reached a state of self-sufficiency. The automobile industry produces an average of 150 vehicles per day in peacetime and 370 vehicles in wartime. The shipbuilding industry has recently shifted its focus from tonnage to increasing speed. Yang concluded that Italy's strength is due to Mussolini's dedication to the party and the nation, his selflessness, and his efforts to strengthen the country. Italians regard Mussolini as a deity, and his smile brings joy, while his anger brings fear. The entire nation's joys and sorrows are linked to him. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

National Government Announces

Supplementary Measures for Shipping Organizations 60

(Nanjing) The National Government issued an order on the 21st, promulgating the Supplementary Measures for Shipping Organizations. This order stipulates that (1) All steamship or civilian shipping companies should organize trade associations and join chambers of commerce in accordance with the Law on Industrial and Commercial Associations and the Law on Chambers of Commerce. (2) Steamships or civilian ships that have not established companies but have been officially registered with the government may use their registration number as a unit to participate in the trade association. (3) The region of a steamship or civilian ship trade association, in addition to the provisions of the Law on Industrial and Commercial Associations, should include companies whose routes span two or more provinces, counties, or cities. These companies should join the trade association in the location of their headquarters. If the company has branch offices, they should also join the trade associations in their respective locations. If there are fewer than seven businesses in the local trade or no company has been established, they may join the trade association in any county or city along the route. (4) The highest supervisory body for steamship or civilian ship trade associations is the Ministry of Communications. Matters concerning the establishment, dissolution, and organizational structure should be submitted to the local government for approval by the Ministry of Communications and reported to the Ministry of Industry for record. Major matters concerning maritime administration should be directly reported to the Ministry of Communications for handling. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

The British-American exchange rate opened at $5.11125, a decrease of 0.025 from yesterday's closing rate. The exchange rate fluctuated slightly in the morning. The final price was $5.110625, a decrease of 0.000625 from the opening price. One US dollar is equivalent to 3 shillings, 10.961 pence.

British-French Exchange Rate: The opening price for the London-French exchange rate was 77.59 francs, an increase of 3 points from yesterday's price. It then fell by 6 points to 77.53 francs.

American-French Exchange Rate: The opening price in New York was 6.59375, an increase of 0.00375.

Tibetan Army Offends Kang

Major Crisis for Sichuan-Xikang Army 82

Financial Difficulties, Soldiers Starving and Freezing

Relaying Official Documents and News Depends Solely on Horseback Messengers

Ya'an Communication: The recent situation of the Tibetan army offending Kang has been telegraphed to the Central Government by Liu Wenhui, Commander-in-Chief of the Sichuan-Xikang Border Defense, requesting financial and material assistance, and requesting that telegrams be forwarded to Qinghai and Yunnan provinces, instructing them to send troops to attack the flanks and rear of the Tibetan army on a specific date to achieve a pincer effect. According to the latest report on the war situation from the Sichuan-Xikang Border Defense Headquarters here, the Tibetan troops recently crossed the river in secret, using more than 500 Dagginbas as the vanguard and about 500 regular Tibetan troops to surround the Dengke County seat. The Kang army garrison in Dengke immediately retreated to the Maliu Lama Temple and resisted desperately. On the 15th, the main force of the Tibetan army crossed the river from Dege. The troops were promptly dispatched by Zhang Worong's regiment of the Sichuan-Xikang army. On the 16th, the Tibetan troops between Dengke and Dege were repelled. On the 17th at noon, the Dengke County seat was retaken. It took several hand-to-hand combats to maintain the original position. The main force of the Tibetan troops then concentrated on Guanyin Temple. The Sichuan-Xikang army launched several fierce attacks, but all failed. Zhang's regiment then urgently dispatched two mortar companies and one mountain gun company from Wuge to assist in the attack. At the same time, reinforcements were sent to the front of Dege. On the morning of the 17th, the Tibetan troops who had forcibly crossed the Jinsha River were defeated, and many leather boats were sunk. At present, the two sides are still facing each other across the river, and the sound of guns and cannons is endless. The Tibetan troops in southern Kang are also showing signs of advancing. According to confidential reports, the main force of the Tibetan army is currently advancing along the Jinsha River and has drawn civilian troops from central Tibet to send to the front to assist in the war. Changdu Garpon Zhen Dongque will personally go to the front to command military affairs. It is heard that their military plan is still based on the expanded military conference held in Changdu last time, and they have decided to attack Xikang from both the north and south simultaneously. If the Sichuan-Xikang army intends to make peace, it must completely cede Dege, Ganzi, Zhuwo, and the villages west of the Ba'an River, hand them over to Tibetan jurisdiction, and unconditionally allow Dagginbas to return to the temple as soon as possible, otherwise it will be difficult to stop the war. All meetings are refused to participate. For the sake of self-defense, the Sichuan-Xikang army has already been strictly vigilant along the Jinsha River and has mobilized militias from Bairi, Ganzi, Luhuo, and other counties to go to the front to assist in the war. However, the Sichuan-Xikang army has limited troops and lacks both funds and ammunition. Currently, only one regiment of Zhang Worong's troops is at the front in northern Kang, and only a part of Ma Chenglong's troops are in southern Kang. Although both regiments are nominally called regiments, they are actually seriously undermanned. The commander of the Xikang Reclamation Command, Tang Ying, and the brigade commander of the 2nd Infantry Brigade, Deng Xiang, in addition to repeatedly sending urgent telegrams, immediately mobilized the Yan Chen Fu San battalion stationed in Guan Nei to leave the Pass as soon as possible and go to the front to defend against the enemy. Battalion Commander Yan Zhicheng has already led the machine gun and artillery companies to the northern route since the twelfth day of the previous month. Battalion Commanders Chuan Dequan and Chen Yuejiang led their troops to the southern route as soon as possible on the 23rd and 24th. In recent years, Xikang's tax revenue has sharply decreased, and military and administrative expenses have all been supported by Sichuan Province. Since Liu Wenhui's retreat to Ya'an, his troops have had difficulty supporting themselves. During the Lunar New Year, loans were issued for military pay, and each brigade received only 1,000 yuan. This shows the financial difficulties of the army. The troops stationed in Kang have been in the icy and snowy land for a long time, and are suffering from hunger and cold. Although Tang and Deng have repeatedly appealed, requesting assistance, Liu Wenhui has no way to think of it. The Ma Chenglong troops stationed in Ba'an were once without food. Recently, with the outbreak of the Kang-Tibet war, at a time when people are needed, the soldiers' salaries are still unsettled. The day before yesterday, each camp was ordered to leave the customs, but they were not paid a penny. Moreover, Xikang is full of mountains and steep roads, and the journey of thousands of miles is extremely painful. There are more than 20 stations from Kangding to Dege, about 1,000 miles. A round trip takes more than a month. The soldiers are extremely tired after traveling along the way. The local grain and tax revenue of the counties outside the pass is only enough to pay for administrative expenses. In recent years, the Tibetan army has stationed troops in Kangding, and the Yi people have been hesitant about paying land taxes. The garrison troops have long been worried about the difficulty of military food. Once a large number of troops are added, food is bound to cause panic. Unfortunately, if the war drags on, there are even more hidden worries. Most counties outside the pass do not have postal services, and the areas with postal services have only one delivery every ten days, which is extremely slow. The original telegraph had wired communication, which could directly reach Ba'an in the south and Changdu in the north. In the 7th year of the Republic of China, the telegraph lines and materials were completely destroyed. The Sichuan-Xikang Border Defense Headquarters had previously installed a wireless radio in Ganzi to communicate military news. Last year, it was ordered to be removed, resulting in all official documents and news relying solely on horseback messengers. Adding shifts day and night, it still takes at least six or seven days from the front of Dege to Kangding, which makes the military command during wartime extremely difficult. The above are all major crises in the current Kang-Tibet war. Commander-in-Chief of the Sichuan-Xikang Border Defense Liu Wenhui has also considered this, but in addition to requesting assistance from all parties and hoping that Qinghai and Yunnan provinces will provide support, there is no other way. (China Joint News Agency)

New Japanese Army Stationed in Tianjin

The Arrival of Commander Umezu 83

Former Commander Nakamura Will Soon Return to His Country

Tianjin Dispatch: Former Commander of the 8th Division of the Japanese Army stationed in Tianjin, Kōtarō Nakamura, originally planned to return to his country last month. However, due to the holding of a large-scale military exercise, his departure was postponed to this month. His successor, Yoshijirō Umezu, departed from Tokyo on the 14th of this month, traveling to China on the Japanese mail ship "Changcheng Maru." On the 19th of this month, at 8:00 AM, the ship entered the port with the tide and docked at the Japanese military camp pier in Tanggu. Due to the shallow water of the Hai River, it could not sail further inland. Therefore, Umezu transferred to the "Hiji Maru" steam launch and sailed to Tanggu. More than 70 people welcomed him at the port, including Japanese Army Staff Officer Miura, Consul General Kurihara, Administrative Committee Chairman Yamahira, representatives of the Veterans Association, and representatives of the Resident Association. All of them had arrived the previous evening. At 9:00 AM, the launch sailed along the Hai River from Tanggu, arriving in Tianjin at 1:50 PM. Because they were waiting for the opening of the Wan'guo Bridge, it was not until 2:00 PM that they sailed to the Mitsui & Co. pier in the Japanese Concession and docked. After the launch stopped, the welcoming party escorted Umezu ashore. At that time, military attachés from Britain, the United States, France, Belgium, and Italy stationed in Tianjin, leading military bands and teams, along with Japanese veterans and students, numbering over a thousand, all stood at the pier to welcome him. Former Japanese Army Commander Nakamura took the lead, stepping forward to shake hands with Umezu, and introduced him to the military attachés of various countries. In order to comply with international etiquette, our side also sent representatives and a provincial government band to participate in the welcome. Subsequently, led by Kikui, the Chief of Staff of the 8th Division, Umezu rode on horseback through Miyajima Street, Akiyama Street, and Fukushima Street, reviewing the troops. The entire Morimoto Regiment of the 8th Division participated in the parade. At 2:40 PM, he entered the Heguang Temple Barracks. The Japanese residents scheduled a banquet at the Japanese Concession Hall at 3:00 PM on the 21st to bid farewell to Nakamura's return to his country and welcome Umezu's arrival in Tianjin. Umezu will take office at noon on the 20th. Two weeks later, he will go to various places in Luandong to inspect the stationed troops, and will also go to our Gubeikou and Xifengkou to inspect. Nakamura is scheduled to leave Tianjin at 9:00 AM on the 22nd, board a ship at the Mitsui Pier, go directly to Tanggu, and then take the "Changcheng Maru" back to his country (19th).

The Northern Route Army Captures Tai'ning 84

Bandits Retreat to Jianning

Nanchang Dispatch: Tai'ning, Shaowu, Jianle, and the cities of Nancheng, Lichuan, and Nanfeng in eastern Jiangxi have long been occupied by Fang Zhimin's Pseudo 9th Army Corps and Luo Binghui's Pseudo 12th Army Corps. When the Eastern Route Army, consisting of the divisions of Lu Xingbang, Leng Xin, and Sun Yuanliang, advanced southwest from the northeast and recovered Shunchang and Jianle, the Northern Route Army, consisting of the divisions of Fan Songfu, Fu Zhongfang, Li Yusen, and Xiao Qian, also advanced southeast from Lichuan and Nanfeng, capturing Jianning and Tai'ning, and coordinating with the Eastern Route Army to achieve the effect of a pincer attack from the east and west. According to news from the Headquarters, aircraft reported that the Northern Route Army had indeed captured Tai'ning County on the 19th. The Red bandits who had been entrenched there retreated in disarray towards Jianning and Ninghua. After capturing Tai'ning, the Northern Route Army immediately established close contact with the Eastern Route Army, coordinating the operations in eastern Jiangxi and northern Fujian. The two large armies from the northeast can cross the border area between Jiangxi and Fujian and advance simultaneously towards western Fujian and southern Jiangxi. (19th)

Following the Earthquake in Wuhan, a Hurricane Struck

Unprecedented in Decades 85

Land and Water Transportation Disrupted, Sheds and Huts Swept into the Air

Numerous Cases of Wall Collapses Causing Injuries, Prisoners Taking the Opportunity to Escape

Hankou Dispatch: Since the beginning of spring in Wuhan, the weather has been chilly. On the 18th, two earthquakes suddenly occurred, and the climate changed abruptly, becoming hot and dry, almost to the point of switching from fur coats to summer clothes. People knew that a major storm was coming. On the 19th, light rain drizzled until 4:00 AM on the 20th, when heavy rain suddenly began. At 8:00 AM, a violent hurricane struck from the northeast, plunging the residents of the three towns into a state of terror. By 11:00 or 12:00, the force of the wind intensified, like ten thousand horses galloping, like a raging tide erupting. On land, rocks were split and cliffs collapsed; on the water, there were terrifying waves. The usual wind speed is 0.2 meters per second, and the maximum wind speed is only 7 meters per second, but on this day, the wind speed reached 9 meters per second. It was truly a,

Hurricane Unseen in Decades. The Yangtze River, both upstream and downstream, and various places in northern Hubei all experienced this storm. Wuhan suffered the greatest losses. When the wind was at its strongest, in the back streets and outside the railway, makeshift huts were mostly swept into the air, spinning and dancing, numbering no less than several hundred. Older residential buildings were also blown down, causing numerous injuries. Several archways on the street of the National Products Exhibition were blown away and fell directly into the river. The Qingchuan Pavilion, a famous scenic spot in Hanyang, built by Fan Zhizhen in the Ming Dynasty, facing the Yellow Crane Tower across the river, also had its roof blown off. Hundred-year-old trees in Gusao Village were uprooted. A high wall of the Wuchang Local Court Detention Center collapsed for over 40 feet. One hundred and six prisoners in the Li Zi Hao prison took the opportunity to escape, resulting in one death, five injuries, and over thirty escapes. More than twenty were later recaptured, and nine major criminals escaped. At that time, pedestrians on the street could not stand firm, and ships on the river were prohibited from crossing. More than ten small boats on the Xiang River risked crossing, but all capsized. One-third of the telephone lines were damaged, especially along the river and inside and outside the railway. The wired communication along the Yangtze River and in the Suizao Tianshan area had its lines broken, making it impossible to report. Wireless communication was also affected by excessive air pressure. The Water and Electricity Company stopped supplying power for two hours due to fires on Jiasheng Road and Siguandian, but fortunately the fires were extinguished before they could spread. Otherwise, the foreign concession would have been turned into ashes. Transportation in the three towns was disrupted by the storm. Flights between Shanghai and Hankou, and Chongqing and Hankou were also delayed mid-route. The Shanghai-Hankou flight was grounded in Jiujiang, and the Chongqing-Hankou flight was grounded in Yichang. Neither could proceed. At 4:00 PM, the wind gradually subsided, and the weather turned cold. The two Public Security Bureaus in Wuhan dispatched many people that evening to investigate the damage in various places in order to provide relief. The general public was greatly relieved, but the refugees living in makeshift shelters had no roofs over their heads. (20th)

Ping City

Ancient Cypress Trees Stolen and Felled 86

Over Three Hundred and Thirty Trees Stolen and Felled

Central Government Dispatches Personnel to Investigate the Truth

Ping Dispatch: The case of the stolen and felled ancient cypress trees in various altars has been taken very seriously by all sectors. The Central Government also considers the matter to be of great importance as it relates to cultural relics and has ordered Committee Member Zhang Ji to come north to investigate the truth so that the matter can be handled strictly. At the same time, the Control Yuan has also ordered Le Jingtao, who is staying in Ping, to investigate the matter nearby so that he can file an impeachment and hand it over for disciplinary action. Yesterday, a certain gentleman from the Antiquities Preservation Committee spoke about the latest situation in this case, saying that newspaper reports have repeatedly mentioned the situation in the Temple of Heaven and the Temple of Agriculture, but it is not known that 42 trees have also been stolen from the Temple of the Sun, 41 trees from the Temple of Earth, and over 40 trees from the Dawuzhai (this place was the former residence of Emperor Yongzheng of the Qing Dynasty, with magnificent architecture, but it has recently been completely demolished, and the bricks, tiles, and wood have been completely sold). The number of stolen trees is even greater than in the Temple of Heaven, with 69 trees in the inner courtyard and 21 trees outside the courtyard (totaling over 330 trees in all the altars, each worth more than 500 yuan). According to a report received by the Committee, a local farmer surnamed Sun said that the cypress trees in the inner courtyard were all living trees that required two people to hug, but now not a single one remains. Of the 21 trees outside the courtyard, more than ten were also living trees. Now the Temple of the Moon has been leased to Hongda College as a school site, and school buildings are currently being built. The foundations are all in places where cypress trees were planted, and the roots have all been dug up. There are still more than ten roots exposed on the ground in the open space south of the northern dormitory. The Committee previously sent personnel to the Western Suburbs Police Station to inquire about the situation, but the police station refused to cooperate. It is not known why. Later, another person was sent to question them, but no information could be obtained. The pine and cypress trees in the temples and altars of Ping City were planted during the Yuan and Ming dynasties and have a history of five or six hundred years. They are of great importance to cultural relics, scenery, and the city's appearance. If this case is not thoroughly investigated, this trend will spread, and the ancient cypress trees of Kaifeng City will disappear. (18th)

The Xihu and Suchang Roads Will Commence Construction 87

The Construction Department Has Appointed the Director of the Engineering Office

The Xihu Highway is of great importance to transportation. The entire line is approximately 130 kilometers long. It is reported that the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department estimates that the construction will require over 1 million yuan. In addition to the 40% loan from the National Economic Commission, the remaining amount has been borrowed from Shanghai merchants, and a draft agreement has been prepared to allow them to invest in transportation. A formal agreement will be signed soon.

It is reported that a section of the Suchang Highway in Changshu has been built into an earthen road that is barely passable. With slight improvements, it can be used. However, a section in Wuxian has not yet been built. The Construction Department has sent personnel to survey and estimate that completing the bridges, culverts, and earthen road will cost approximately 140,000 yuan. In addition to the Wuxian County Government being able to raise 70,000 yuan from the county's various construction funds, the remaining amount is planned to be borrowed from Shanghai merchants.

It is reported that the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department has appointed Mei Chengzhang as the Director and Engineer of the Xihu Road Engineering Office, and Yu Liji as the Director of the Suchang Road Engineering Office. They will soon begin to organize the Engineering Offices and plan the work.

Frequent Fire Alarms in Urban and Rural Areas

Songjiang 88

On the evening of the 18th of this month, the Qia Yuan Yang Workshop west of the Ta Bridge was destroyed by fire, which spread to nearby houses. Fortunately, the Third District Fire Brigade rushed to the rescue, averting a disaster. This morning, at dawn, Zhang, who lives along the railway at Dongxing Bridge, had three thatched sheds built. He had saved up a little money over the years and had prepared wood to build tiled houses. This morning, while cooking snacks, he knocked over a kerosene lamp onto a pile of firewood, causing a fire. In an instant, the three firewood sheds were reduced to ashes. The fire was extinguished after various dragon boats rushed to the rescue.

Fifty Coffins Reduced to Ashes

Changshu 89

The Xiku area near the Ouchu outside the East Gate of this county was once a rural village, but in recent years, more and more people have moved in, turning it into a desolate cemetery. There are nearly fifty coffins in the area, making the scene even more desolate. The day before yesterday, a woman surnamed Lu returned to Changshu from Shanghai. It was approaching the Qingming Festival, so she went to Xiku to sweep the tomb. However, she was careless when burning paper money, and the fire spread to the coffins, reducing nearly fifty coffins in the area to ashes. Among them, several coffins had not been buried for long, and the corpses had not yet decomposed. After being burned, a foul odor filled the air. The nearby residents discovered the fire and went to extinguish it and pursue the old woman surnamed Lu, but she had already returned to Shanghai and could not be found.

A Family in Guijiashi Was Robbed in the Morning 90

In the Gaomuqiao South area of Guijiashi, District 12 of this county, Xu Haida, a villager who is in his fifties, had a relatively well-off family, which attracted the attention of bandits. At 3:00 AM on the 19th of this month, six bandits suddenly came, all armed with wooden sticks and single knives. After entering the house, they immediately grabbed and beat Haida, forcing him to reveal where he had hidden his silver. Xu had no choice but to tell them everything. As a result, he was robbed of fifty yuan in cash and miscellaneous items worth about one hundred yuan. The victim has reported the incident to the Public Security Bureau and requested that the bandits be apprehended.

A Quack Doctor Swindles a Large Sum of Money

Wuxi 91

Yang Letian, a resident of this county, has lived in Shanghai for many years and resides in the Airen Lane on Avenue Road. Recently, he used the methods of a quack doctor to swindle Ms. Dai Baoru, who lives in Shanghai, out of 8,900 yuan, and forged a deposit slip for 2,000 yuan from the Luzhen Da Yang Goods Store. Initially, he said that it was deposited in the Luzhen Da Yang Goods Store in Xiaoshatu, but the owner of the store, Lu Zhicheng, testified that it was forged. Yang then changed his story, saying that it was from Luzhen Da in Wuxi. The lawyer representing the plaintiff, Ye Fukan, sent someone to Wuxi to investigate. Yang's original home is Jiangxi Bridge, and there is no Luzhen Da Yang Goods Store there. There is also no Luzhen Da Yang Goods Store in the urban area. The investigator returned to Shanghai yesterday to report to lawyer Ye so that he can report to the First Special District Court tomorrow during the court session and strictly punish him according to the law.

A Dispute Over Ancestral Graves Leads to Suicide by Hanging 92

Next to the Songzi Temple on Mount Hui in this county, there is a Zhang family cemetery that has been there for decades. This spring, Zhang Shougen and Zhang Abu, who lives in Taiping Lane, have been fighting over the ownership of the cemetery property. Each has his own story, and there is no resolution. The day before yesterday, Shougen suddenly filed a lawsuit in the County Court, accusing Abu of seizing property rights. Abu, upon hearing the news, did not know what to do and suddenly had thoughts of giving up on life. Yesterday morning (the 21st) at around 1:00 AM, he hanged himself on a tree in the Shang surname cemetery in Xumen Xu Lane on Mount Hui. It was not until after dawn that someone noticed him. He had already died. Zhou Tingquan, the Zheng of the Twenty-Two-Five Tu, and Yan Xieying, the Zheng of the Twenty-Two-Nine Tu, reported the matter to the County Court, which sent Prosecutor Shen to lead officials to conduct an autopsy. It was determined that he had died by hanging. The corpse was ordered to be prepared with coffins and collected.

Three People Poisoned to Death by Eating Pufferfish Roe

Danyang 93

Wang Zixia, a migrant living in a thatched shed near the Dukou Bridge north of the city, made a living selling sugar. The day before yesterday, Wang Zixia found pufferfish roe near the railway station and brought it home to cook. In the evening, he ate it with his children and invited Xu, the wife of his neighbor Xu Wu, to eat with them. However, Wang's family was poisoned after eating it. Wang and his wife were the most severely poisoned and died one after another. Xu, upon hearing the news, rushed over to inquire, but soon became numb all over. Xu Wu, knowing that his wife had been poisoned, tried to rescue her, but was unsuccessful. She also died. Wang's children were less severely poisoned and survived.

The Baojia System Must Be Completed by the Deadline

Zhenjiang 94

In order to complete the organization of the people's self-defense capabilities and eliminate bandits, the Jiangsu Provincial Government has decided to first implement the Baojia system in the counties north of the Yangtze River. It has issued orders to the counties to comply. Now it has ordered that it be completed within four months. It is reported that after Governor Gu returns to the province from Jiangxi, he will personally go to the counties to supervise the progress.

The Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department Admits Engineering Students 95

In order to recruit talent, the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department has organized an engineering personnel selection committee. Over 800 people have registered. After the committee's review, 190 people were qualified in civil engineering, 16 in mechanical engineering, 10 in electrical engineering, 1 in electrical and mechanical engineering, 1 in electrical and civil engineering, and 14 in other engineering fields. The grades are divided into four levels: first-level deputy engineer, second-level assistant engineer, third-level engineer, and fourth-level supervisor. Currently, ten people, including Peng Yumo in civil engineering, have been hired. The rest will be hired one after another.

Frequent Bandit Cases in Urban and Rural Areas

Nantong 96

Recently, there have been frequent bandit robbery cases inside and outside Nantong City. Xu Mingyuan's home in Pingchao Wujie Bridge was robbed by bandits on the 18th, and his six-year-old grandson was kidnapped. The County Government, seeing that bandit cases have been frequent in the county, has ordered the police to strengthen patrols and set a deadline of two weeks to solve the case.

Coastal Fishermen Request the Suppression of Bandits and the Protection of Fisheries 97

The spring fishing season is approaching in the coastal areas north of the Yangtze River, but piracy is rampant. Representatives of fishermen have submitted a request to the province to suppress bandits and protect fisheries. A Village Outside the Embankment Was Robbed and Murdered

Qingjiang 98

On the night of the 14th, many bandits suddenly came to Heshang Village outside the East Embankment of Huaiyin, broke into Ge Wenju's house, and swarmed inside. Wenju and his eldest son, Jietian, resisted slightly and were shot by the bandits. One bullet hit Wenju in the head, causing his brains to spill out, and he fell to the ground and died instantly. One bullet hit Jietian in the leg, causing him to lose his ability to resist. The bandits then looted at will and took Wenju's youngest son, Jieqian, and his nephew's wife, Jia, away. However, they released Jia halfway. According to Jia, after being released on the Yellow River beach, the bandits fled north of the Yellow River. On the 15th, the family carried Jietian to the Ren Ci Hospital for treatment and filed a report with the County Government requesting an autopsy and requesting the rescue of the kidnapped boy.

A Lantern Show Turns Tragic

Funing 99

Various agencies and organizations in this county held a lantern show for the National Products Movement last night and tonight. Unexpectedly, the lanterns were crowded last night, and the road was blocked. A worker from the Renshou Pharmacy, who was only fifteen years old, was pushed down by the crowd, and his stomach contents were trampled out, causing serious injuries. A person surnamed Ge from Yangzhai Town fell into the water and died when returning to his boat after watching the lanterns. The family members heard the news and came to the city to cry bitterly. A child surnamed Wang from Dongxiang went missing and was only found this morning. County Magistrate Li Jinfang, in view of this, ordered the Public Security Bureau today to prohibit the lantern show from being held tonight. Some stubborn lantern enthusiasts were very disappointed upon hearing this.

The Qinzhen Changban Ferry Causes an Accident

Gaoyou 100

The Zhen Tong ferry of Qinzhen Changban collided with a heavy load of green bean ship passing by the Qingshuitan yesterday (18th). Because they could not avoid it, the ferry was accidentally sunk. Fortunately, the shipowner and crew were rescued, the shipowner complained to the ferry to claim for all losses.

A Male Corpse Was Discovered in Dongquan Pond

Jiashan 101

A male corpse that appeared was found in Dongquan Pond, Jiashan county, yesterday. He was about thirty years old, wearing a black coat, a blue silk gown, and had a hemp rope tied to his body, with a huge stone below. The corpse has already rotted and seemed to have been murdered and thrown into the river. The local village police are working on collecting the body

Three Fire Alarms in One Day

Hangzhou 102

Hangzhou City has been experiencing dry weather lately, and fire alarms are frequent. Three fires broke out on the 19th, one in the morning and two in the afternoon. (1) A fire broke out at the home of Ding Lianchang, a resident of No. 11 Xianglu Yuan outside Wulinmen, due to carelessness while brewing wine. Fortunately, the fire was quickly extinguished, but five houses were burned down, causing a loss of over 1,000 yuan. (2) At around 4:00 PM, a fire broke out at the Hoji Ice Factory on Datong Bridge Street outside Wangjiangmen. The fire brigade rushed to put out the fire, which was extinguished at 5:00 PM. It is estimated that two ice storages were burned down, causing a loss of about 3,000 yuan. The arsonist, Zhu Youfu, has been detained by the Bureau for questioning. (3) At 6:00 PM, a fire broke out at the home of Wang Heshang, a resident of No. 44 Hongmen Bureau, due to carelessness while cooking dinner. Fortunately, the fire brigade was able to rescue the situation, and no major disaster occurred. The loss was still minor.

A Platoon Leader Who Seduces and Rapes a Civilian Woman is Sentenced to Imprisonment 103

Hu Xiong, a platoon leader of the 9th Company, 3rd Battalion of the Zhejiang Security Department Infantry Regiment, seduced Xiu Ying, the daughter of Ding Xu, a civilian woman, while working as a clerk at the Jinhua Recruitment Office in July of last year and brought her to Quzhou in September. Ding Xu filed a complaint everywhere. Director Yu was furious, and Hu Xiong had already been selected to study at the Military Academy. He was ordered to be detained by the academy and brought to justice. After investigation, the facts were confirmed, and he was sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment.

A Tragedy Occurs During a Play Performance at the Qichimiao Temple

Shaoxing 104

On the 19th, the locals in Qichimiao Temple in Shaoxing Hujiang Township initiated and hired the Shengban Yangchun Stage to perform women's drama. Men and women in silk and satin flocked to watch, and the temple was packed. At about 12:00 AM, the stage behind the temple, which had been in disrepair for many years and had been eroded by wind and rain, suddenly collapsed with a bang, and the entire building collapsed completely. As a result, more than a dozen male and female actors and spectators were crushed. After the rescue, it was found that all had broken heads and broken feet. Among them, the male actor Xu Guantang and the female actor Ren Qiuqin died instantly due to severe injuries. The other injured people were also in critical condition and were sent to the city for treatment. Wang Jian, the village police officer, reported the incident to the court and asked Prosecutor Zhao to conduct a rural examination on the afternoon of the 21st.

Meningitis Spreads Through Cities and Villages

Xiaoshan 105

Recently, the weather in Xiaoshan County has been uneven, and there has been little rainfall, resulting in meningitis outbreaks in various places. Over twenty people have died from the infection in Dongmenwai Zhuanba Xinlin Zhou and Xixing Changhe Wenyan. There is a lot of work going on treating patients with needles in the Xiaoshan hospital. On the 19th, the Lu family, a merchant in Wenyan Xiabu, lost four members to the illness. All of them suffered from acute meningitis.

Careless Farmers Burned to Death Two Children 106

On the night of the 19th, a fire broke out in the home of Zhang Huijin, a farmer in the Shalangyu area outside the West Gate of Xiaoshan, due to a careless stove fire. In an instant, ten flat houses and nine thatched houses were burned down. In addition to the household items being destroyed, two young children of the Yu family, aged five and three, were unable to be rescued and were buried in the fire, their heads and faces scorched beyond recognition. It was a terrible sight.

The King of Johor (i.e., the Sultan) of the British Malaya Federation, Sultan Ibrahim, and his wife and a group of six people, who are traveling around the world, the King and Queen of Johor (photographed by Xi Shuxian)

came to China by way of the Japanese ship Fushimi Maru on the 12th. Details of Arrival 108

I.'s Statement 109

He plans to transfer to the Taiyo Maru on the 24th to travel east. He will visit Japan for two weeks, and then take the Chichibu Maru to the United States in the middle of next month. Then he will cross the Atlantic Ocean, travel to various countries in Europe, and return to Johor. I. will stay in Shanghai for three days and is scheduled to take the Japanese ship Taiyo Maru to Japan on the 24th for sightseeing. On the 12th of next month, he will take the Chichibu Maru to the United States from Japan.

Chairman Wang Xiaolai reported, saying: "Ladies and gentlemen, today is the opening of our Nanshi National Products Market. We are honored to have Representative Cai from the Ministry of Industry, Mayor Wu of Shanghai, Director Wu of the Social Bureau, and veteran comrades from the Party-state and the national products industry to grace us with their presence and guidance. This market has been in preparation for several months, and fortunately, it has received the unanimous assistance and enthusiastic participation of various national products manufacturers. On behalf of the association, I would like to express my sincere gratitude. The sole purpose of the Nanshi National Products Market is to promote national products. The first objective is to promote the patriotic spirit of the people. Because in recent years, foreign goods have flooded the country, especially in Shanghai, which has the most. It has almost made the people of the whole country only know that foreign goods are good, and our national goods, even the good ones, have become inferior. This is really a major problem for the people of the whole country. Therefore, our association, knowing this situation, feels it is really terrible. In addition to setting up a product exhibition hall and the Beishi Tianhou Temple Bridge National Products Market, we have specially set up this Nanshi National Products Market to let the citizens of Shanghai, both north and south, know that there are purely superior national products that can compete with foreign goods. The second is to develop the national economy and the people's livelihood. The national economy and the people's livelihood were mentioned in the Three People's Principles of the Premier. In short, it is that national products are developed, and the development of national products means the revitalization of industry, so that the people's livelihood problems can be solved. The third is to increase the international trade position of our country. I have checked the customs trade statistics in recent years, and the imports have exceeded the exports every year, and last year was particularly serious, it can be said that the ratio of ten to one. Therefore, to promote international trade, national products must be developed, and they must be carefully studied, especially the materials, decoration, and prices must be given full attention. The above three points are of great importance. I hope that all of you present here will work together and keep them firmly in mind and follow them. As for the preparatory process, please ask Director Wang to report."

Mayor's Speech 115

Next, Mayor Wu Tiecheng gave a speech, saying: "Today is the opening of the Nanshi National Products Market of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and guests from all walks of life are quite crowded. This proves the great patriotic consciousness of the general public. However, to promote national products, we should also use national products. It is not only effective through verbal propaganda. If everyone can use national products as much as possible, the dumping of foreign goods can be stopped, loopholes can be plugged, and the country's prosperity can be expected. I hope that our citizens will all follow this ambition, so as not to betray the purpose of propaganda and promotion."

Preparatory Process 116

Next, Wang Yansong reported on the preparatory process, saying: "Today, our association's Nanshi National Products Market is holding its opening ceremony. We are honored to have guests from all walks of life. Our association has always taken promoting national products as its mission. In the tenth year of the Republic of China, we established a product exhibition hall near our association, collecting the essence of domestic products for the reference of all walks of life. We have held various industry product exhibitions and temporary national products markets for more than seven times. Later, in the twentieth year of the Republic of China, in view of the influx of imported goods, our country's national products were almost completely destroyed. And with the prosperity of the Shanghai market and the establishment of shops, it is rare to find a completely national products market, so that those who love to use national products still do not know what to do. Therefore, our association deeply knows that the goods in the exhibition hall are not only for reference, but also need to be purchased. Therefore, we immediately set up a national products market in the original site of the exhibition hall, which can not only arouse the determination to use national products, but also promote the actual effect of promoting national products. Since its establishment, the business has been very developed, which shows that our people are not without patriotism, but really feel that there is no real national products market. Moreover, this year is the Women's National Products Year, and we must work harder to promote national products. Therefore, we added the Nanshi National Products Market at the old site of the former County Chamber of Commerce on Zhonghua Road, Xiaonanmen, Nanshi, so that the residents of Nanshi area can feel the convenience of purchasing and using national products. After several months of preparation, it was finally completed. The organization of this market is exactly the same as the national products market in the original product exhibition of our association. In order to make the whole market perfect, each factory in the market is limited to one, and no similar products are allowed to be mixed in. And the selection of national products is extremely careful, and the arrangement and layout are all in line with beautification. The house of this market used to be the old site of the County Chamber of Commerce, and then it was lent to the Social Bureau for use. The internal situation was not suitable for business. Therefore, we hired workers to repair and rebuild it, and renovated the facade to create a grand view. Also, at the beginning of the preparation of the association, we appointed Mr. Yang Zhenxin as the general manager, responsible for carrying out everything, and sent staff to take charge of various affairs to complete it. As for the participating factories, there are more than 30 companies, including China Enamel Factory, Apuer Electric Appliance Factory, Qiming Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Wuhe Weaving Factory, Huafu Hat Factory, Huahua Silk and Satin Bureau, China Chemical Industry Co., Ltd., Heji Food Company, Du Jinsheng Silk Weaving Factory, Guangdong Brothers Rubber Factory, Shengsheng Ranch, and China National Products Company. In the future, they will definitely arouse the interest of the Nanshi people in using national products, create a great cause for the national network, and give a great blow to foreign goods. Also, this market has also received generous donations from various national products factories, which will be distributed to guests and customers, and the old brand national products Apuer Electric Appliance Factory will supply all the light bulbs at half price. Their enthusiasm is deeply appreciated. I would like to thank all the factories on behalf of this market, and hope that all of you present today will use your usual patriotic spirit to strongly promote and guide us, and especially hope that the public opinion circle will vigorously advocate and promote us, so that our national products will make endless progress and keep pace with imported goods. In the Hurricane and Fog the Day Before Yesterday

Niuzhuang Steamer Runs Aground 122

Two Holes Broken in the Yangtze River Estuary

Ship Sent to Help Rescue and Repair in Shanghai

The afternoon before yesterday, a strong wind occurred in Shanghai, and there was also fog on the sea. The Niuzhuang Steamer of the Taikoo Company in this port ran aground in the Yangtze River estuary due to the invasion of strong winds and fog, and the ship was badly damaged. The Shanghai Office received the news and has sent a ship to tow and rescue it. The reporter of this newspaper immediately conducted a thorough investigation after receiving the news. The details are as follows:

Encounter with Wind and Fog 123

The Niuzhuang Steamer weighs 2,480 tons and sails to various ports in the north and south. This time, it carried goods from Tianjin and went directly to Fuzhou to unload. At 11:00 am on the 20th, the ship arrived at the Yangtze River estuary. It was at the time when a hurricane occurred on the sea, and there was thick fog, which made navigation very difficult. The captain intended to anchor there to avoid it temporarily, but unexpectedly the fairway was blocked by fog,

Runs Aground and Damaged 124

The ship had not yet anchored and was still sailing. Unexpectedly, it had hit a reef, and the bottom of the ship was broken, with two holes. Seawater immediately entered the cabin. Fortunately, the cabins of the ship were separated by iron plates, so that it would not affect the entire ship. The captain immediately ordered to drive at full speed and sail to the nearby shallow beach, so that the ship would not sink. When it was driven to the shallow beach four miles west of the Yangtze River estuary, it stopped to wait for rescue.

Emergency Telegram for Help 125

The captain immediately reported to the Shanghai Office by wireless, and requested to send a ship to help rescue. The Taikoo Company received the telegram from the ship and first telegraphed the Ganzhou Steamer, which was on its way to Shanghai, to go to the place to help and check the damage. Yesterday morning (i.e. the 21st), the Shanghai Office sent the Huatong Small Steamer to Shanghai to load engineers, cement wood, and various ship rescue equipment, and rushed to the Yangtze River estuary to help repair the hull and pump out the accumulated water in the ship, etc.

Can Arrive This Morning 126

In the first step of emergency rescue work, the two holes broken by the reef in the Niuzhuang Steamer were first repaired with cement, and then efforts were made to tow it to Shanghai for repairs. The reporter asked the company in the afternoon and was told that the Niuzhuang Steamer had run aground and was being rescued. It is expected that it can be towed to Shanghai for repairs this morning (i.e. the 22nd). As for the passenger and cargo soaked in the water in the ship, the details are still unknown and will be inspected after the ship arrives in Shanghai for unloading.

Sanbei's Jianglun

Hongli Runs Aground in Hunan 127

Yongkang Went to Tow and Rescue

Still Unable to Haul Out

Sanbei Company's Hunan shipping industry is the crown of the six companies. There are currently four Hong-character Jianglun ships that travel back and forth. This time, the Hongli ship transported goods from Shanghai to Hunan, which was the first ship to Changsha after the upstream water rose. The goods carried by Hongli were mostly cotton yarn. The ship's draft was very shallow, and the load was only about eight feet, so it seemed that it could pass without any problems this time to Hunan.

The Ship Runs Aground 128

Unexpectedly, the ship suddenly ran aground on the river near the lower mud port near Changsha. The hull was deeply mired in the sand. The captain tried every means on the spot, but could not escape from the shallow beach. He had to send a telegram to Changsha and Hankou to request a ship to rescue. The place where Honghe ran aground was considered to hinder the Changsha waterway. Therefore, after the accident, the Changsha Customs also sent personnel to monitor the towing and rescue.

Sent a Ship to Rescue 129

The Hankou Branch received the report and immediately telegraphed Shanghai and immediately sent the Yongkang ship to tow. The Yongkang ship used the thickest and strongest steel wire rope to put on Hongli, and Yongkang towed it at full speed. But Hongli was heavily loaded and mired in the mud, and was aground very deeply. It was impossible to tow it out for a while. When it tried its best to pull forward, the steel wire rope was broken, and Hongli still could not be rescued.

Haul Out After Discharging 130

Now the cargo owners in central Hunan, because the goods in the Hongli ship have been blocked on the ship for a long time, hinder the market business, so the cargo gangs and the Sanbei Company Branch consulted and decided to unload the cargo in the Hongli ship onto barges first and transport them to Changsha. Now the Yongkang ship is sent to tow five barges to Xiani Port, to the side of Hongli, first unload the cargo inside the ship and transport it to Hunan, and then wait for the water to rise before towing and rescuing.

Fulong Damaged 131

The company received a telegram from Nanjing yesterday that when the Fulong ship was docked at the company's wharf in Beijing, the Changan ship, which was used for dispatch, was also berthed outside the wharf. At that time, the northwest wind was very strong, and the tide was high. The hull of the Changan ship squeezed into Fulong. At that time, the cabins, stairs, etc. of Fulong were all damaged, and the anchor chain was also broken, and the iron anchor fell into the water. This matter has been discussed and resolved peacefully by the office of the ship management office and the Beijing office of Sanbei Company.
