Huang Shaoxiong and Dai Jitao took the night express train to Beijing last night.

Page 11

Public Concession Public Works Bureau

Resolved to Rectify Rickshaw Measures 133

Adopted the Recommendations of the Joint Meeting of the Police and Transportation Committees

The Public Works Bureau's Board of Directors meeting on the afternoon of March 21 discussed the joint meeting of the Police and Transportation Committees. It drafted measures to rectify rickshaws and decided to adopt the recommendations of the joint meeting to establish a rickshaw management office, and appoint two Chinese staff and one foreign staff to be responsible for it. The powers of the office are to report to the Board of Directors, cancel or issue (to groups or individuals) rickshaw licenses. The number of public rickshaw licenses is still limited to 10,000. It also has the power to issue or cancel rickshaw puller licenses. The number of public rickshaw pullers is limited to four times the number of rickshaws. For private rickshaws, one person per rickshaw, and cannot issue more without sufficient reason. Regarding the fourth to sixteenth recommendations of the Investigation Committee, which have been reviewed and approved by the joint meeting, are now adopted by the Board of Directors as follows: 1. The management office may make suggestions at any time to gradually reduce the number of licenses. 2. The rickshaw owner registration book, as recently compiled, should be put into effect immediately. 3. Both public and private rickshaw pullers should be licensed, and the methods should be drafted and implemented immediately. 4. The maximum rent for public rickshaws is eight dimes per 24 hours, and pro rata for less than 24 hours. The rent schedule is to be drafted by the Public Works Bureau. The license regulations should stipulate that the rent is not allowed to exceed the amount allowed by the Public Works Bureau. 5. The fare should be two dimes per mile and six dimes per hour. The fare schedule should be posted in a conspicuous place on the rickshaw. 6. Public rickshaws should be improved immediately. 7. Vehicle inspection should be carried out more strictly than before. 8. The rickshaw lamps should be thoroughly improved. 9. Rickshaw parking places should be set up at convenient locations in various places, and regulations should be formulated. Anyone who hires a rickshaw must strictly follow the order of hiring. 10. Before changing the methods, regarding the rickshaw puller license regulations, the current public and private rickshaw license regulations, and the methods and time of issuing licenses, should be reviewed by the relevant departments of the Public Works Bureau and reported to the Board of Directors for implementation. 11. Those who hold a private rickshaw license should indicate the vehicle number and their name on the rickshaw puller's license. If the rickshaw puller is changed, it should be re-indicated immediately. 12. The police department should continue to crack down on "wild chicken" chartered cars. 13. The Public Works Bureau should contact the French Concession and the municipal government authorities to cooperate in order to improve the conditions of public rickshaws.

The committee also suggested that the Public Works Bureau should clearly state that all rickshaw licenses and magnetic badges are the property of the Bureau in perpetuity and are only lent to the license holders for use on a timely basis. Any private sale of licenses will not be recognized. Any transfer of licensed rickshaws must be approved and registered by the Bureau. Rickshaw owners who wish to cease operations must report to the Public Works Bureau. All applications for continued licensing must be considered by the Bureau. This proposal was also adopted by the Board of Directors.

The Investigation Committee found that passengers often ask rickshaw pullers to wait in the central district, but regulations do not allow parking, so the rickshaw pullers may not be able to get their fare or may be interfered with by the patrolmen due to stopping. This behavior puts the rickshaw pullers in a difficult position. The public should be notified to pay the fare immediately upon alighting. This suggestion was also adopted by the Board of Directors.

Rickshaw Merchants

Explanation of Rent Reduction Opinions 134

Letter to the Public Works Bureau

Yin Zhiling, Liang Yangting, Gu Songmao, Xia Muyao, and Zhu He Gao, the executive directors of the Rickshaw Association's Special Zone Office, submitted a document to the Public Works Bureau, stating: "In order to consider the fundamentals, we have drafted a reduced rent schedule and attached rickshaw industry forms, requesting your review. We have previously submitted a report from the Bureau's Vehicle Committee, and in addition to questioning the suggestions, we have paid attention to and prepared for all the reform and improvement items. As for the rent reduction, we have now collected opinions and listed the vehicle costs and operating income items separately as forms, and discussed them repeatedly. The existing rent really needs to be reduced, but we are afraid that the amount proposed by the Vehicle Committee will be difficult to implement. Therefore, based on a compromise method, we have drafted that the daily rent for public rickshaws will be reduced to twelve dimes in the future, as a way to consider the fundamentals. Therefore, we explain it as follows: (1) Appropriately reducing the rent is not only the demand of the rickshaw pullers, but also recognized by the rickshaw owners. However, helping rickshaw pullers is not entirely about reducing the fare, but about increasing their intelligence. It is found that when rickshaw pullers earn a fare, they will definitely spend it all, and when they earn very little, they will definitely use old tricks to owe rent to the contractors. The nature is like this, the habit is like this, everyone knows it. At best, even if the rent is not charged, it is impossible to save money. (2) If the daily rent is actually reduced to eight dimes, the position of the contractor should be removed. The rickshaw owners and the contractors have contracts with a fixed term of years, which should be legally binding and cannot be changed halfway. Even if we take a step back and allow them to be eliminated, the contractors have no business to run. The rickshaw pullers usually borrow money and owe rent, and they will definitely be pursued one by one. The places where they usually live will definitely be evicted immediately. If the rickshaw pullers cannot cope with it for a while, it is inevitable that unnecessary disputes will arise. In short, reducing the rent is originally an urgent task. If we do not consider everything and go our own way, it will not only be unfavorable to the rickshaw owners and foremen, but also there will be various difficulties for the rickshaw pullers. Therefore, the association, in the midst of a compromise rent reduction, is building hospitals to treat the rickshaw pullers' illnesses, building new villages to make the rickshaw pullers live comfortably, and making model rickshaws to make it easier for them to pull, and setting up training centers to increase their knowledge, and all other matters that should be set up and prepared are gradually carried out. Once it is completed one day, the actual effect will be fully achieved, then it will not be difficult for the rickshaw pullers to pull the rickshaw directly to the rickshaw owners. Once the rickshaw pullers can pull the rickshaw directly, the rent price proposed by the Vehicle Committee will be realized at that time, which is a natural trend and there is nothing to worry about. If we want to implement this rent price immediately, it is not only impossible to take care of both the standard and the original, but also if we use it to help the rickshaw pullers, we are afraid that it will only be a name but not thorough. We have specially listed the reasons for drafting the daily rent reduction to twelve dimes, and the vehicle costs and operating income items separately as forms, and submitted a document to request your review. If there is anything appropriate, we ask you to reply and follow."

Public Works Bureau

Warned Qinfeng Factory Yesterday 135

The Factory Requested the Machinery Association to Intervene According to Law

Qinfeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory at 546 Baoding Road has a considerable history in the dyeing and weaving industry run by Chinese people. The Public Works Bureau of the Public Concession suddenly sent a letter to the factory yesterday, saying that all the internal equipment of the factory did not meet the requirements for factory use, such as the facilities in the boiler room, raw material room, and weaving places, which were detrimental to public safety. In order to take care of public safety, it should immediately find ways to improve it, otherwise move out to maintain safety, etc. After receiving this warning letter, the factory believed that when the factory was first established, it must first be reviewed by the Engineering Department of the Public Works Bureau. Only after the review was suitable could it be opened. Now that the Public Works Bureau has approved it in the past, how can it be said that it is not suitable? It immediately requested the Federation of Mechanical National Products Factories to intervene according to law.

General Assembly Declaration 141

The association also issued a declaration yesterday, stating: "A country cannot stand without its people, and the people cannot progress without unity. The late Dr. Sun Yat-sen said, 'Our people are like a heap of loose sand. Without organization, how can we survive?' Alas, if all the people of our country can understand this principle, then it is not too late to mend the fold after losing the sheep. The citizens of Shanghai have been bathed in the culture of civilization for the longest time and have undergone the tempering of revolution for a long time. Everyone is willing to make every effort for the benefit of the country and the people, and they will also not hesitate to sacrifice everything to resist those who invade our land and sovereignty and seize our property and lives. During the 'January 28th' Incident, this association once organized a citizens' volunteer army to bravely fight against the enemy, and organized refugee shelters to help the poor. Other examples include enthusiastically donating goods and supplies, wholeheartedly providing vehicles and clothing, assisting military affairs, maintaining the market, regulating finance, and mediating commercial affairs. All the facts have long been made clear to the world. Although it can be said that it is the inherent duty of our people, it is also sufficient to prove the association's pragmatism and willingness to sacrifice. However, in recent days, people's livelihoods have become more difficult, the country's steps have become more difficult, foreign disasters have been frequent, and internal strife has not ended. The covenant of the League of Nations is as if it does not exist. Arrogant and powerful neighbors have become the hosts and seized the territory. The lost territory in the Northeast has not been recovered, and the unrest in Xinjiang and Tibet has come again. Chen Jigong has retreated to southern Fujian, and Sun Dianying has risen again in Ningxia. Foreign goods are dumped, and the agricultural villages in various provinces have gone bankrupt. National goods are sluggish, and the Shanghai market is even more depressed. Alas, we, looking at the state affairs, already feel extremely frightened. Can Shanghai, which claims to be the richest in the country, still witness its demise and not help each other? Now, the third representative assembly of this association has been established in accordance with the regulations. Learning from the past, strengthening unity, burning our boats, and having no turning back, we will uphold the friendship of helping each other in the same boat, show the sincerity of saving ourselves and others, support the government, promote people's livelihood, lead public opinion of citizens, complete the foundation of autonomy for the country, and restore the prosperous city. Therefore, we declare our intentions and hope that all compatriots and gentlemen will carefully consider them."

Mr. Maze Requests Leave to Return Home 143

Departing April 1st

Mr. Maze, the Inspector General of Customs, has been in office for over ten years and has had no spare time to return home once. Due to the recent heavy workload and mental exhaustion, he urgently needs to return home for a short rest. Therefore, he has specially requested the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance for six months' leave, which has been approved by the authorities. He will take a ship back to England on April 1st to visit relatives and take care of personal affairs. In 1927, while serving as the Customs Commissioner of the Jianghai Customs, Mr. Maze once requested leave to return home. However, due to his important position and the lack of a suitable replacement, it was not approved. Since Mr. Maze took office as the Inspector General of Customs in 1929, his official duties have become even more numerous and pressing. Now that the national customs administration has entered a regular track, and each department has its own commander, he is taking the time to rest. Although Mr. Maze is a foreign advisor, since his promotion to important positions, he has eliminated the previous abuses of foreign power over Chinese authority. All customs personnel and administration are under the command of the Chinese government. He focuses on handling matters within his duties, planning carefully, and implementing necessary reforms without complaint. Therefore, customs revenue has increased several times compared to the past, and domestic and foreign credit has been maintained, which is relied upon by China's finances. In the past two years, he personally went to various places to investigate and prevent smuggling, which has greatly benefited the national treasury. Other achievements include the improvement of the treatment of Chinese employees and the equal status of Chinese and foreign employees. Many Chinese officials have been promoted to important positions, all thanks to Mr. Maze's leadership. Currently, while Mr. Maze is on leave to return home, his duties will be temporarily assumed by Mr. Rocherfort, the current Customs Commissioner of the General Affairs Department. The position of the General Affairs Department will be assumed by Mr. Ding Guitang, the current Chinese Secretary. The position of Chinese Secretary will be assumed by Mr. Lu Bin, who is currently in the United States studying the customs administrative system. Mr. Lu has been summoned to return home and is expected to arrive in Shanghai in early April.

After Mr. Hawke arrives in Shanghai, he will go to Hangzhou to fly the Condor aircraft he brought from the United States, perform in Shanghai, and make a long-distance flight between Shanghai and Hangzhou.

Chinese Merchants

Cigarette Factory Conference Revises Tax Rate 147

Since the Zhongmin Cigarette Company and others proposed the revision of the tax rate, there has been no concrete plan, which has caused many misunderstandings from all parties. The cigarette factory industry is also in a state of anxiety. Previously, the industry association convened a joint meeting of executive and supervisory committee members to discuss the plan. It was resolved to send a letter to the proposer Huang Ziping, asking him to quickly summarize the opinions of the proposal, draft a practical plan, and then pass it on to the next executive and supervisory committee meeting for discussion, so that it can be submitted to the government to ensure that tax revenue is not reduced and that Chinese factories can receive real benefits.

Shanghai Yearbook Publication Postponed 148

The first Shanghai Yearbook (1933) was highly praised by all parties. The second (1934 edition) has been thoroughly revised and was originally scheduled for publication at the end of March. Now, the Shanghai Yearbook Society has issued a notice postponing the publication date to the end of April. According to the editors of the society, the reason for the delay is that after various manuscripts were typeset, various new materials were continuously searched. In order to seek new and accurate results, the editors successively withdrew the manuscripts from the printing house for addition and replacement. Many special contributors also acted cautiously and repeatedly withdrew the original manuscripts for revision, resulting in slowness in typesetting. In addition, because the page numbers of each column in the first yearbook were listed separately, it was inconvenient to check. This time, the total page number of the entire book is increased, which must be completely typeset before the code can be printed, which is also one of the reasons for the slow publication.

Machinery Association Petitions the Ministry of Railways

Correcting the Discrepancies in Freight Charges on Two Railways 149

The Same Steel Enamelware

Shipping to Beijing is More Expensive than Shipping to Hangzhou

The Shanghai Machinery-made National Goods Factory Association submitted a document to the Ministry of Railways yesterday, stating: "We are presenting a matter regarding the discrepancies in freight charges on the two railways, please correct. We have found that the steel enamelware manufactured by the factories of the association members, the freight from Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway to Hangzhou is calculated according to the third-class product per kilogram. If it is transported from the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway to Beijing, it must be calculated according to the second-class product per meter, resulting in a sudden increase in freight by more than double. Both are state-owned railways under the jurisdiction of your ministry, but the grading of goods is different, and the discrepancy in freight is so great. Moreover, since the joint transportation was completed, each box of steel enamelware transported from Shanghai to Qingdao, if handed over to the railway for joint transportation, costs 19 yuan, and it only costs 5 yuan for sea transportation by foreign ships. The association is a national goods organization and will definitely support the development of joint transportation, hoping to reduce leakage. We usually repeatedly urge the member factories not to hand over transportation to foreign ships in order to comply with the principle of national goods being transported by the nation. However, in terms of freight, the foreign transportation is so light and the railway is so heavy. The discrepancies in freight and the different grading between the Shanghai-Nanjing, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways are even more shocking. It is reasonable to prepare a document for presentation, requesting your ministry to review and correct it, so as to benefit the railway transportation of national goods and avoid foreign ships encroaching, which is truly for the public convenience."

Xujiahui Installs Water Pipes

French Municipal Council Interferes Beyond Its Borders 157

Demolishing Water Pipes and Expelling Guards

Merchants and Residents of the Whole Town Rise Up in Opposition

Since last winter, the Shanghai Municipal Government approved the installation of tap water pipes in Xujiahui Town by the Public Utilities Bureau to meet the needs of residents. However, the French authorities claimed that the road section from the Yang Baokang Rice Store in front of the intersection of Xuzhen Road, north along Haige Road to the intersection of Tongren Street, about 20 yards long under the sidewalk, was built beyond the border. Therefore, they did not allow water pipes to be laid underground there, causing a part of the project to be invisibly stalled. To this day, it has not been resolved. Unexpectedly, at around 9 am the day before yesterday (19th), during the busiest time of business, French patrolmen suddenly dispatched 10 armed Chinese and Vietnamese policemen, with great momentum, and ordered the vendors there to move away and not to set up stalls. They also expelled the second post police of the sixth district of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who had been stationed there for years to maintain traffic in the center of the road, and did not allow them to stand there. The police, unable to communicate in their language and fearing misunderstandings, reported to the police station. After receiving the report, the station chief Bi Zhenhua believed that it was related to national sovereignty and it was difficult to remain silent. In addition to ordering the police to temporarily serve at the street intersection (i.e., the intersection of Xuzhen Road), he reported the information to Director Wen, who forwarded it to the Municipal Government to make serious representations to the French Consul. At about 2 pm, the French Municipal Council dispatched a Westerner leading dozens of workers to forcibly demolish the section of water pipes that had already been laid and dug them out from underground and piled them on the wasteland west of the Tongren Street Bridge. People were panicked and uneasy for a time, causing major diplomatic conflicts. Merchants and residents of the entire town believe that the land there belongs to the Chinese territory. Now the French Municipal Council has unreasonably driven away our vendors, seized our police power, and is taking every inch. If we do not fight for it on the basis of reason, what unimaginable consequences will there be in the future? It is said that an emergency meeting will be held at a certain number in the town this afternoon to discuss countermeasures, and they are willing to be the government's support.

Yesterday's Jackson Ship

Arrest of Japanese Offender Yamauchi 158

Yesterday, the Japanese-language Shanghai Daily reported that the Shanghai Japanese Consulate Police Station received a telegram from the Waseda Police Station in Tokyo on the 19th, stating that a passenger, Kyohei Yamauchi, had committed the crime of abduction and embezzlement and escaped to Shanghai on the President Jackson ship. They hoped to arrest him immediately. However, since the ship was owned by the United States, the Japanese police station consulted with the US Consul General, and with the Consul General's consent, at 6:30 this morning (21st), two officers, Ito and Koyuen, led the officers of the Municipal Council to board the ship and arrest the offender. (The offender had already used the alias Kiyoshi Nakata on the ship.) According to the offender's confession, he graduated from the Faculty of Law at Tokyo Hosei University and is currently serving as the secretary of the First Finance Bank of the Tokyo Credit Association. On March 14th, after embezzling over 2,000 yuan from Mr. Ozawa, he secretly escaped to Shanghai. The reasons for his crime are quite complicated, the most important being a woman problem. At the time of the arrest, he still had over 1,700 yuan in cash with him.

Poor Hong Zhengqing

Suicide After Unemployment 159

Seeking Work for Over a Year, Ultimately Unsuccessful

Wife's Search Hastens His Death

Hong Zhengqing, a native of Ningbo, was 41 years old. He used to work in a money exchange. His family consisted of his wife, Yu, 43 years old, and six children. Lacking any permanent assets, the family relied entirely on Hong's earnings. He lost his job nearly a year ago and frequently traveled between Shanghai and Ningbo, seeking recommendations from relatives and friends for work, but without success. Recently lodging in a hotel, he felt overwhelmed by the burden of supporting his family, leading to thoughts of ending his life. He attempted suicide multiple times but was stopped by relatives and friends. They sent a letter to his wife, Yu, requesting she come to Shanghai to supervise him or accompany him home. His wife arrived in Shanghai after receiving the letter.

She stayed for only three days, lodging at the home of a relative surnamed Yuan at 98 Kulun Road, Zhabei, and asked people to find Hong. However, upon learning his wife had come to Shanghai to find him, Hong became even more determined to end his life. On the 19th, at 11 PM, he went to the Youfa Small Hotel at 154 West Xinjiao Street in the French Concession, renting room number four. That night, he ingested poison and committed suicide. The next day at noon, a hotel worker, Zhang Jinsheng, was cleaning the room and asked him to get up, but received no response. He pried open the door and found that Hong had taken poison and was unable to speak. A suicide note was on the table in front of the bed, addressed to his wife and children, and his brother-in-law, Yu Lanqing, bidding farewell and asking them to take care of his wife and children. The hotel immediately reported to the police, and he was taken by car to Renji Hospital. Treatment was ineffective, and he died at 2:30 PM. The hospital notified the police, who sent detectives to the Tongren Fuyuan Sub-hall to examine the body. The family was notified. Yesterday morning, a report was filed with the Second Special District Court, and Prosecutor Wang Ren arrived to examine the body, confirming that the deceased had died by ingesting poison. His wife was allowed to claim the body for burial after signing a guarantee.

Dispute Over Giving Up a Seat on the Tram 160

A University Student Gives Up His Seat to a Chinese Woman

Unexpectedly Taken by a Western Woman

| A Minor Dispute Arises, the Western Woman Accuses Him of Injury |

Zhu Erkang, a student from Shanghai's St. John's University and a native of Ningbo, was on his way home from school on the morning of the 15th of this month at 10:15 AM. He boarded a Route 1 bus and it was quite crowded. Suddenly, Huang Xucai, a female teacher at a Municipal Council primary school, boarded the bus with her nanny, Zeng Pengshi, carrying a child. Zhu immediately stood up and offered his seat to Zeng Pengshi. However, a Western woman, Kraeler Cher, who was sitting next to them, suddenly took the seat and gave it to another Western woman, Peidi Peggy. Zhu negotiated with her, leading to a dispute. A ticket inspector named Leve Ming caught wind of this and took both parties to the Jing'an Temple police station. After investigation by the detectives, both parties were released. Afterwards, Kraeler suddenly went to the German doctor, Bai Li, for examination, claiming that her head and fingers had been injured by Zhu's beating. Dr. Bai issued a medical certificate. Kraeler then reported the incident to the police station, who then asked the First Special Court to issue a summons. Zhu was summoned to court yesterday morning. The police lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, filed charges according to Article 293 of the Criminal Law. Kraeler Cher and Peidi Peggy Leve testified that Zhu Erkang indeed punched Kraeler's head. However, Zhu denied it, saying, "I asked them to stand up, and the plaintiff immediately uttered abusive words and hit me repeatedly. I never hit the plaintiff at all." Subsequently, Huang Xucai and Zeng Pengshi came forward to testify, saying that they only saw the plaintiff beating the defendant and did not see the defendant beating the plaintiff. Judge Wu Xiangzu then ordered the plaintiff to be examined by a forensic doctor. The results showed that Kraeler only had a minor scratch on her middle finger, and no other injuries. Judge Wu then ruled that Zhu Erkang was not guilty. The police requested that he be released on bail during the appeal period. The court then instructed Zhu to provide a surety who could be summoned at any time during the appeal period.

Woman Dies from Tooth Extraction 161

| A Quack Doctor Causes Immeasurable Harm |

In the Pingyin Bridge area of Xietu Road, Shanghai, a woman from Anhui, Liao Zhang, 35 years old, suffered from severe tooth pain, causing her to be unable to eat or sleep. She hired a quack doctor named Sun Zhen to treat her. Sun said the tooth needed to be extracted. He forcibly pulled out a molar with pliers. Unexpectedly, he injured a blood vessel, and the bleeding would not stop. The woman immediately fainted and died shortly after. Notification from the French Municipal Council

Measures to Prevent Gas Light Leaks 162

Rooms Should Be Equipped with Safety Devices

Fuel Residue Should Be Removed Outdoors

The Director-General of the French Municipal Council in Shanghai, Chuan Leisi, issued a notification yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of notification, gas lights, even if they do not contain carbon dioxide, already have toxic properties. If they contain carbon dioxide, the toxicity is even greater. Therefore, any gas leak can cause a major disaster. This bureau hereby warns all gas users to take preventative measures to avoid chronic poisoning or suffocation, and to prevent the gas from mixing with oxygen in the air and causing an explosion. Those who use gas for heating must know that gas can produce carbonic acid and carbon dioxide, which is the same as using charcoal. Therefore, the residue from this fuel must be removed outdoors at all times, otherwise it will cause harm, even if it does not lead to death. As for rooms with gas equipment installed, each unit should be equipped with a vent. The sealed hot water tank of a gas water heater should be equipped with safety devices. The surface of the tank that comes into contact with the flame should be cleaned at least once every two years. This notification is hereby issued."

According to Bao's confession, the Guangfeng Company had planned to fire Zhou last year because his cooking was poor, which angered Zhou.

Origin of the Robbery 165

The company's joint account, Gongyu Money Exchange, lacked accomplices, so he discussed it several times with Bao, Xiaomazi Zhou Huansheng, and Huosun Lin Gen at Bao's home. Later, Xiaomazi gathered accomplices to commit the robbery. Afterwards, Xiaomazi gave Bao 100 yuan of the stolen money. At that time, Zhou thought it was a good idea, so he deposited 2,700 yuan with Yang, and Yang gave him another 700 yuan, instructing him to entrust it to Huosun Lin Gen, and to distribute 500 yuan to Zhou Xiaotao and 200 yuan to Bao Azhang. Municipal Council

Annual Report of the Music Band 169

The report of Mr. Mei Baiqi, the leader of the Municipal Council Music Band, for the past year states: "Six special concerts were held this year, with audiences ranging from 1,100 to 1,837 people. Regular Sunday concerts were held at the Carlton Theatre seventeen times before May, with an average audience of 385 people. After October, nine concerts were held at the Grand Theatre, with an average audience of 666 people. Twenty-nine open-air concerts were held in the summer at the Zhaofeng Public Garden. The brass band performed in various parks thirty times.

The structure of the Grand Theatre seems to be very suitable for sound films, but not very suitable for the performance of the music band. Moreover, there are no suitable seats on the stage, so the arrangement of the performers is difficult to be appropriate, and the lighting is also not perfect. As for the performance time, some people strongly advocate changing it to 5:15 PM on Sunday afternoons, instead of the current 9:15 PM, to facilitate the audience.

Chinese people are paying more and more attention to the performances of this band. This year, a Chinese musician participated in one of the special concerts, and the results were very satisfactory. Although the general audience is not large, the number of Chinese people among them is increasing, especially in the summer.

From January to May last year, the band was broadcasted by radio, but the results were not very satisfactory. This year, a new broadcasting method has been arranged so that the public can enjoy the band's performances without paying for tickets."

Public Concession

Overview of Public Utilities 178

The Municipal Council's annual report includes reports on various public utilities. Here are some key figures:

The total consumption of tap water last year was 1.6 billion (1,600,000,000,000) gallons. This amount of water is enough to cover the entire area of the Public Concession to a depth of more than ten feet. The maximum consumption in one day was 57 million gallons. The amount of water used per hour in the summer mornings reached 3.5 million gallons.

The electricity company currently has 73,642 customers. The total amount of electricity supplied throughout the year was 753,568,000 units (kilowatts). The maximum supply in one hour was 133,134 units. There were 5,314 public streetlights and 6,390 private streetlights.

The telephone company had a total of 49,401 telephones installed at the end of the year, an increase of 4,796 from the previous year. Since the establishment of the temporary agreement for the areas outside the concession, 850 telephones have been installed.

The tram company currently has 17 tram and trolleybus routes: 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 8, 11, 12, 14, 15, 16, 17, 18, 19, and 20. In 1932, the trams traveled a total of 9,407,656 miles and carried a total of 108,845,656 passengers.

The gas company had 13,380 customers last year and sold a total of 755,717,000 cubic feet of gas. The amount of coal used to produce gas was 52,590 tons.

Wu Guobao Invents Automobile Parts 185

Increasing Load Capacity and Avoiding Shocks

Automobile manufacturing expert Wu Guobao, a Cantonese, studied mechanics in the United States and interned for many years at major automobile manufacturing plants in that country, gaining considerable knowledge. He is truly a rare talent in our country. After returning to China, Mr. Wu, noting that the transportation vehicles used by the Chinese army were the same as those used for ordinary transportation in cities, which was unsuitable for military use. Urban automobile transportation has specific regulations, weight restrictions, and smooth roads, making travel convenient. However, when it comes to military use, transporting heavy objects such as military equipment and shells, these vehicles are not applicable. Mr. Wu has now invented a mechanism that, when installed on these transportation vehicles, can increase load capacity and avoid shocks. Mr. Wu is now drawing up plans for his invention and submitting them to the National Government for registration and patenting.

After discussion and resolution by the public, it was passed. A re-election of directors and supervisors was held. Yuan Ruifu, Cao Guohua, Jiang Junyi, and others were publicly elected as four ballot counters. The election results were announced, and Wu Zhihao, Xiang Shengwu, Lin Kanghou, He Shaoyu, Wu Zhihe, Zhou Yongsheng, Cao Guohua, Chen Cuifu, He Shaoting, Dong Zhongxiu, and Zhuo Yuting were elected as the eleven directors. Yuan Duanfu, Zhuang Songfu, and Lu Qisheng were elected as the three supervisors. The meeting concluded at six o'clock."

Raging Waves Sink Cargo Ship 191

At about 7 p.m. the night before last, during a heavy wind and rainstorm, a pier boat belonging to local Chen Gengsheng, loaded with 1,000 bags of buckwheat and root flour, was docked outside the Huizhou vessel at the Taikoo Wharf in the French Concession, waiting to unload its cargo. At that time, raging waves surged incessantly in the river. The boat was overloaded, and large waves crashed onto the deck, instantly sinking the boat and its cargo into the water, resulting in significant losses. Afterward, the boat owner reported the incident to the customs and water police for record.

Director of the Pudong Fusheng Hospital

Visits the China Mental Hospital 192

Returns with Dr. Jiang, Director of the Hongkou Pingdeng Clinic

The China Mental Hospital, located next to the Xiaocai market on Dongyouheng Road, Hongkou in this city, was founded in 1912 and specializes in treating various kinds of madness and all kinds of difficult mental illnesses. Its reputation is widespread. Recently, Qian Le, director of the Pudong Fusheng Hospital, suddenly heard of the hospital's great reputation and came to Shanghai with Dr. Jiang Benyi, director of the Hongkou Pingdeng Clinic, and others to visit the hospital. The hospital's medical director accompanied them on a tour of the entire hospital and explained the various facilities in detail, such as the rubber safety rooms, continuous bath, electrotherapy room, mental patient observation room, and screen atmospheric therapy. Qian praised the perfect equipment, which could be compared with the Angcheng Psychiatric Hospital in Paris, and the quiet location and pleasant scenery, which are especially suitable for recuperation. It is truly the only mental hospital in China, and it is not an exaggeration. They then took pictures to commemorate the visit and bid farewell.

Decrease in Court Observers 193

Those Without Observer's Passes Will Not Be Allowed to Enter the Court

Guo Yunguan, President of the Shanghai First Special District District Court, noting that the civil and criminal courts of the court are extremely crowded with observers during daily trials, and that the quality of the people is mixed, if not properly restricted, not only will the order of the court be affected, but it will also be insufficient to prevent problems. Therefore, after discussing with Shen Jiayi, President of the Second Branch Court of Higher Court, he decided to strictly implement the observer's ticket system. A public notice has been issued in recent days, informing all kinds of people that, except for news reporters who have long-term observer's tickets, all others must obtain temporary observer's tickets before they are allowed to enter the court to observe. Yesterday was the date of implementation. The court authorities ordered the iron gate along Qipu Road to be closed, and all those going to the court were uniformly directed to enter and exit through the main gate on North Zhejiang Road. The number of guards at the gate was increased, and all those who came to the court were questioned one by one by the guards. If they were litigants or those who wished to observe, they were instructed to first obtain an observer's ticket at the ticket issuance office located to the left of the main gate, otherwise they would be prohibited from entering the court. After this restriction, the number of observers in each court has been greatly reduced compared to before. However, those who stood and watched outside the court gate all day were suddenly crowded.

The Chen Youliang Case Still Has Many Doubts 194

Conclusion of Arguments Withdrawn

On August 15, 1931, a case occurred in the Fashang Hotel at No. 113 Xinxiao Bridge Street in the French Concession, where Jiangbei bandits opened fire and brutally killed their fellow bandits, killing Jiang Zhonghan, Xia Yongsheng, and a man surnamed Xue, and injuring Zhong Ziqing. The Public Security Bureau arrested the murderer Yan Jinbiao, who was sent to the Second Special Court for sentencing to death. After three trials, the sentence was finalized and he was executed in April. However, the mastermind confessed by Yan was Li Guocheng, a native of Funing, also known as Chen Youliang. Yan's family members handed him over to the Public Security Bureau, and the Second Special Court brought him back and prosecuted him. After several trials, at the end of last year, Li Guocheng was sentenced to death for jointly planning the murder, with permanent deprivation of civil rights. Li refused to accept the sentence and hired two lawyers, Lu Shijie and Shen Yushan, to appeal to the Third Branch Court of the Higher Court. They also presented Ma Buwen, the former captain of the Funing Police Sub-team and the current captain of the Yancheng Police Brigade, and neighbors Chen De'ao and Chen Bizhao as witnesses. The High Court has held one or two hearings to summon the witnesses. The trial was concluded, and the sentence was originally scheduled to be announced yesterday. However, it is now known that there are still doubts in the case that need to be reviewed. Yesterday afternoon, Director Guo, accompanied by Sun and Fan, two judges, held a hearing, brought Li to court, and announced the withdrawal of the conclusion of the arguments. A new hearing will be scheduled and the arguments will be reopened. Li was still sent back to custody.

Arrest of Bandits and Seizure of Military Equipment 195

On the afternoon of the day before yesterday, at 6:20 p.m., Chinese and foreign detectives from the Jiaxing Road Public Security Bureau arrested two bandits, Wang Desheng, a native of Zhenjiang, and Zhao Zhengfu, a native of Jiangbei, in Room 23 of the Yong'an Inn on Maignan Road. They seized a Mauser pistol, 19 bullets, handcuffs, and a letter of appointment and took them into custody at the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Wang Yaotang, the lawyer of the Public Works Department, stated that the investigation revealed that the defendants and Wang Da Sizi, Xiao Sizi, and a person surnamed Ding, who are at large, were planning to rob a household on Xinzha Road. The pistol was obtained by Wang through illegal means. He requested a postponement for detailed investigation. The gun and bullets were presented for inspection. Wang Desheng confessed that he met Zhao while working at a certain yarn factory and invited him to chat at the inn. The pistol was not his. He stammered in his confession. Zhao Zhengfu confessed that he was previously invited by Wang Xiao Wuzi to rob a certain place. He refused to go because he had been prosecuted for previous crimes. That evening, he was invited by Wang Desheng to sit in the inn. He was arrested shortly after. Judge Xiao ordered that they remain in custody and be re-examined at a later date.

A Concubine Tries to Flee

A Coward Commits Suicide in Anger 196

Yu Xuqing, a native of Tongzhou, 51 years old, lived at No. 101 Rugao Lane on Tongzhou Road. He used to be a worker in a cigarette company, but recently he has been unemployed and at home. His concubine, Ms. Chen, 39 years old, although old, is naturally romantic. Seeing Yu's weakness and incompetence, she cannot help but feel disgusted and has found another lover outside. A few days ago, she made the excuse of going out to find business and wanted to move her clothes and belongings away, but Yu discovered her plan and tried to stop her, resulting in a constant quarrel. The day before yesterday, Yu, after thinking about it, felt extremely resentful and suddenly had the thought of ending his life. Before dawn, he went out alone and hanged himself on an electric pole in the lane. At about 6 a.m., he was spotted by his neighbor Mao Zhaotong, who tried to untie him. Unfortunately, he had already breathed his last. He immediately reported it to the Jiaxing Road Public Security Bureau, and detective Liu Shuxun was ordered to investigate. He then took him by car to the Tongren Hospital. The treatment was ineffective, and he soon died. The body was carried to the Feilun Road Autopsy Center. Yesterday morning, he reported to the First Special District District Court, which appointed Prosecutor Guo Wei, accompanied by the two forensic doctors Wei and Zhang, and clerk Wang Zuyi, to come to the center to examine the body. According to the testimony of the deceased's son, Yu Xiaobing, 14 years old, "The deceased is my father. Recently, my mother wanted to run away, so he committed suicide. They had fought each other." According to Yu Chen, a native of Yancheng, "My former husband owed the deceased 60 yuan, and could not repay it, so he gave me to him as his wife. Five days ago, I wanted to make a living, so I moved my clothes to Little Sisters' place on Dalianwan Road, and he argued with me." According to the report of Chinese detective Liu Shuxun, "After the investigation, Guo ruled that the deceased Yu Xuqing had indeed committed suicide by hanging himself before death." The body was handed over to his son Yu Xiaobing, who signed an agreement to take it back for burial.

City News 197

Sichuan Store to Establish a Main Store on Nanjing Road The Sichuan Store in the Paoqiu Stadium of this city has long been famous at home and abroad for selling Sichuan silver ear fungus, all Sichuan products, and ginseng and bird's nest tonics at genuine prices. Therefore, even in this time of economic depression in all industries, the store's business has been growing daily. Recently, the address of the Paoqiu Stadium store is located in a corner, which is not enough for use. It is also not very convenient for customers to come and go. Therefore, it has also established a main store at No. 316 Nanjing Road (East End of Pintang Lane), the most bustling central area of this city. It is currently being renovated day and night. The rules are very grand and will be completed soon and will be opened soon. From now on, it will be more convenient for people from all walks of life to go to the store to buy silver ear fungus.

New Store for Sichuan Silver Ear Fungus Silver ear fungus from Tongjiang, Taiping, and Nanjiang counties in northern Sichuan is the best, and its effects are greater. Local ear merchants have their own mountain farms. The industry in this city has been wholesaling from them for over 30 years. The Xie Xinggong Silver Ear Fungus Shop on Yanghang Street in the French Concession is the organization for these merchants. Recently, silver ear fungus from Guizhou and Hubei has also been transported to Shanghai for sale. In order to maintain the Sichuan silver ear fungus, the merchants have specially contacted the ginseng merchants and established a retail department in the Paoqiu Stadium on Nanjing Road, named the North Sichuan Silver Ear Fungus Shop, specializing in the sale of silver ear fungus, ginseng, bird's nest, deer antler, musk, cinnamon, and various tonics, totaling over 100 kinds, with prices at 10% off wholesale prices. There are ginseng and bird's nest products for one yuan and high-quality silver ear fungus products for two yuan (limited to one can per person), exquisitely decorated, with a guarantee of refund and replacement. It is reported that the shop has opened and its business is very prosperous.

How to Study the Northeast Problem) 2 ( 204

Yesterday, a Mr. Fang, claiming to be a refugee from the Northeast, proposed how to study the Northeast problem and requested the editorial department to pay attention. Now, we will first make a blunt clarification of Mr. Fang's views, and tomorrow we will discuss the methods for studying this problem. - The Editor

We are very grateful to Mr. Fang for raising such a practical issue, which allows us to have the opportunity to re-awaken readers' attention and discussion of the Northeast problem. We have long said that theory and practice cannot be separated. Whether studying social sciences or literature, if you only read dead books and pay no attention to practical problems, then even if you read ten thousand volumes of books, you can only be a bookworm. Therefore, whenever we deal with general problems, we always try to bring up many concrete problems as examples. Of course, this is still not enough, and we should also discuss more specific practical problems as the center. Regarding this point, in addition to fully accepting Mr. Fang's opinions, we also hope that readers will raise more such practical problems for discussion in the future. Regarding Mr. Fang's letter, we can divide it into two parts to answer: one part is based on the current situation in the Northeast as described by Mr. Fang, with a brief explanation; the other part is how to study the Northeast problem.

Let's talk about the first part first. The current situation in the Northeast as described by Mr. Fang is, of course, largely true. Imperialists treat all colonies in this way: they use both high-pressure policies and appeasement policies, which is the most vicious policy. However, from Mr. Fang's letter, we see that Mr. Fang seems to only focus on one aspect of the problem: seeing the temporary prosperity of Manchuria without seeing the hidden crisis; seeing the apparent depression of the people's spirit without seeing the reasons for the depression and the power and anti-imperialist struggle of the hundreds of millions of people lurking within. Undoubtedly, the September 18th and January 28th incidents created absolutely different attitudes among different social groups in China. Some people are indeed "depressed," no! Or more accurately, they are "indifferent," or to put it more harshly, they are very optimistic. They only know how to show off beautiful words and phrases to deceive everyone. Mr. Fang cannot help but feel the vastness of the "songs and dances of peace" at sea, but this does not include the general public. These high-class Chinese have always been like this. Has "golf" and "foxtrot" ever stopped for a single night on the day of January 28th? These places, of course, are not accessible to hardworking people. People who can talk don't do it themselves, and they are probably not happy when others do it. Regarding the anti-Japanese aspect, we have indeed seen many people who want to "resist," using blood to exchange for blood, but at the same time, there are also people who are preventing others from doing it, and who do not hesitate to use "blood" to fight for the victory of this national policy. Naturally, the temporary victory will belong to this group.

Therefore, on the surface, although the national crisis is becoming increasingly serious, the phenomenon shows "songs and dances of peace," the masses are silent, creating an illusion for Mr. Fang.

What about the other group? They cannot afford to play "golf" and cannot afford to "foxtrot." They are suffering in life and have been forced to the brink of death. They have no other way to go except to fight to the death with imperialism. These people are bound to disturb the jazz music in the dance halls. Although sometimes they are forced to be silent, the "bandits" all over the country are being suppressed every day, but the disturbances are still there, and the world is not peaceful. This shows that under the cold crust, there is still a raging fire, and the earth has not really died!

Speaking of the volunteer army's resistance against Japan, we certainly admire the heroic acts of the past, but speaking of the comparison of forces and the purity of quality, the current surviving civilian armed forces are indeed weaker in number than before, but in fact, they are more optimistic than before. Because there were too many high-class Chinese in the previous front. Now that generals have become famous for resisting Japan, they should naturally retire to famous mountains and receive offerings of fragrant flowers. Of course, only the truly fearless "muddle-headed fools" bury their heads in doing foolish things. In this way, although the large "army" has been changed to small guerrilla warfare, it is indeed a bit of a trouble for the Japanese army because these lowly people do not love money and bribes. Therefore, in this aspect, a contradiction is also formed. On the surface, the volunteer army is indeed weakened, but in its essence, the volunteer army is growing and reorganizing. Unfortunately, Mr. Fang only sees the appearance.

In short, the people and things that Mr. Fang saw are all wearing illusions, and they have all been deceived by the smoke screen of the high-class Chinese. Although excited and indignant, it is inevitably filled with the mood of defeatism and the mood of pessimism, as if there is only despair for the Northeast, but this is not the case.

This is a mistake. Of course, we cannot deny the influence of the Japanese imperialist appeasement policy on the people of the Northeast, nor can we ignore the role of slave education on the people of the Northeast; at the same time, we can no longer tolerate everyone being willing to be depressed. But we should also recognize reality and have a scientific and correct analysis of the reality of the Northeast, and liberate the above illusions.

This is undoubtedly a matter of observation methods, which is a problem that people who are concerned about the national crisis must first grasp. Below, we will put forward specific methods for studying the Northeast problem; at the same time, we will liquidate some harmful thoughts of Mr. Fang and many people with the same views as Mr. Fang, in order to contribute to those who are concerned about the Northeast problem and serve as their reference. (To be continued)

Education News

Students of National Universities in Other Provinces

Results of Physical Examination 223

The Physical Strength of Northerners is Not as Good as that of Southerners

The results of the Ministry of Education's physical examination of students from national universities across the country (13 national schools, 9 provincial schools, and 19 private schools in total) are as follows:

According to the results of the physical examinations of students from national, provincial, and private universities across the country, the Ministry of Education has compiled statistics. Among the total number of 13,485 people examined, (1) the development part is divided into three types: A, B, and C. The number of people in type A is 6,166, in type B is 5,649, and in type C is 1,140. (2) The nutrition part is also divided into three types: A, B, and C. The number of people in type A is 5,754, in type B is 4,976, and in type C is 1,365. (3) The average height is 153 to 173 cm. (4) The average weight is 41.5 to 65.0 kg. (5) The average lung capacity is 2,600 to 3,500 cubic centimeters. (6) The average chest circumference is 63 to 88 cm. (7) The average vital capacity is 308.2 cm. (8) The average grip strength is 24.3 to 68.0 kg. (9) Number of people with diseases) (10) Vision part: 1. Nearsightedness in one eye: 215 people, 2. Nearsightedness in both eyes: 1,263 people. (11) The hearing part is divided into three types: A, B, and C. The number of people in type A is 7,788, in type B is 2,811, and in type C is 508. Among them, in the development part of the total number of people examined, 1,097 out of 1,632 people from Peking University were in grade A, and 1,339 out of 1,975 people from Northeast University were in grade A, while only 499 out of 1,608 people from Sichuan University were in grade A, and only 278 out of 1,285 people from Central University were in grade A. It can be seen that the physical strength of northerners is not as good as that of southerners.

Deputy Director of the International Labour Organization

Mo Lei-de Arrives in Beijing to Discuss Cultural Cooperation 226

Lecturing on [French Normal Education] at the Central Government

Mr. Mo Lei-de, Deputy Director of the International Labour Office of the League of Nations, entrusted by the League of Nations' Institute of Intellectual Cooperation, has come to China to investigate labour and cultural conditions and to help develop Chinese education. Mr. Mo arrived in Beijing last week and has been very busy visiting the President of the Executive Yuan, Wang Zhaoming, the Minister of Industry, Chen Gongbo, and the Minister of Education, Wang Shijie. On the afternoon of the 20th, the Ministry of Education specially invited Mr. Mo to the Ministry for a tea party to discuss cultural cooperation. It is said that the main method is to pay attention to the future research direction of Chinese students studying abroad. Because our country is currently experiencing a shortage of talent, various technical personnel are seeking to hire foreign personnel, and at the same time, it is felt that students studying abroad have no way out after returning to the country, resulting in a mismatch between supply and demand. This time, Mr. Mo was ordered to come to China to negotiate with our country's authorities on the establishment of a guidance mechanism between the League of Nations and China to direct the direction of students studying abroad, with the aim of cultivating the talents needed by China. This plan is under discussion and a concrete decision will be made in the coming days. Luo Jialun, President of National Central University, considering Mr. Mo an educational expert, specially invited Mr. Mo to the university the other day to lecture on [French Normal Education]. The following is a transcript of his speech, the gist of which is that before discussing the French normal education system, two special principles of French politics and education should be explained: (1) France is one of the ancient civilizations and had early establishment of universities, the structure and spirit of which still exists in current education. (2) Although France is a democratic country, its history is quite short, and it gradually formed since 1870. From the second principle, French normal education, because it must adapt to the needs of a democratic country, promulgated a law in 1885 stipulating (1) that education is a right that everyone should have; (2) that education is transcendent and not bound by religion; (3) compulsory education for children; (4) free admission to national education. Before the promulgation of this law, only 500,000 children were enrolled in schools nationwide, and after the promulgation of this law, 3 million children were enrolled in schools at the same time. Therefore, there was a sudden shortage of primary school teachers. In order to train a large number of teachers, the country established one primary normal school for both men and women in each of the 89 prefectures, recruiting primary school graduates and giving them three years of rigorous training. This was because, based on the needs of a democratic country, each prefecture established primary normal schools simultaneously within one year. The curriculum of primary normal schools focuses on the inculcation of three points of common sense, the cultivation of hygiene and moral concepts, and the understanding of world social concepts. In addition, there are two higher normal schools, one for men and one for women, in Paris to train teachers for primary normal schools. The curriculum is also based on the above three principles, but the level is raised and the content is enriched. The state attaches importance to normal education, so for education, six to twelve years old is primary education, above is primary normal, and above again is higher normal. The foundation is large and the top is sharp, like a pyramid, very neat and uniform. This is one of the characteristics of French teacher education. As for the training of secondary school teachers, there is no special normal university. Graduates of ordinary universities can serve as secondary school teachers after passing the higher diploma examination. Therefore, the knowledge is very rich, but because they have not received considerable normal training, they feel a lack of teaching methods. This is the second characteristic of French normal education. Although France nominally does not have advanced normal schools for training secondary school teachers, there are two advanced normal schools in Paris. Admission to these two schools is very strict, focusing on the study of specialized knowledge and not on teaching methods. After graduation, some students serve as secondary school teachers, and some continue to stay at the school for three years of research, after which they can serve as professors in various universities. Many senior officials of the League of Nations and many political and diplomatic figures in France have also come from this school. Although this system is quite unique, its advantage is that it emphasizes rationality. Most secondary school teachers obtain excellent teaching methods from experience. This is the third characteristic of French normal education. After Mr. Mo finished speaking, Luo, the president of Central University, stood up and said that European education focuses on in-depth research of knowledge, and American education focuses on teaching methods, both of which are worthy of our reference for educational research.

Peking Research Institute

Excavating Antiquities in Shaanxi 228

Discovering Historical Sites such as Tang Steles and Song Porcelain

Excavations in Daming Palace and Xingqing Palace

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) After it was reported that the Shaanxi Archaeological Society, jointly formed by the Beiping Research Institute and the Shaanxi Provincial Government, had excavated Tang Dynasty Daming Palace and Xingqing Palace illustrations, reporters learned that the director of the society, Xu Bingchang, had returned to Beiping. They visited him to learn more. The following is a record of Xu's conversation:

The current address of the society is in a side courtyard of the Shaanxi Civil Affairs Department, which is the former site of the Qing Dynasty Provincial Administration, and also the former site of the Tang Dynasty Secretariat. Tang steles have been unearthed there many times. In the winter of the 11th year of the Republic of China, the garrison also discovered the Yan Qinli stele written by Yan Lugong in that place, which is now stored in the small stele forest of the Pacification Commissioner's Office. Last year, the Historical Research Association of the Beiping Research Institute sent me and others to Shaanxi for archaeological research. After arriving, we heard people say that when the Yan Qinli stele was discovered, the workers saw several stones under the stele and reported it to the foreman. However, at that time, the foreman could not pay the workers according to regulations because of the soldiers. The more work they did, the more money they lost, so he ordered the workers to hide them. My colleagues and I thought that most of the buried stones in the lower layer were still Tang steles, so we wanted to excavate them. Later, we found the foreman who contracted the work that day and asked him to point out the place where the original stele was unearthed and to ask about the buried stones in the lower layer. Unfortunately, he firmly denied it, so it was stopped. Later, we heard that he had told people in private that this denial was not true. We also heard that when the Yan Qin stele was first unearthed, before it was taken out of the pit, workers had rubbed it out several times, which was the earliest rubbing [the so-called "pit rubbing"]. The current value is quite expensive. My colleagues and I found the worker who rubbed the stele in the pit that day based on this clue and pointed out the pit, but because we were busy, we were unable to start work immediately. In February of this year, when I left Xi'an, because this kind of work did not take much time, I ordered He Shiji and Zhang Jiayi to excavate in their spare time. Now we have received a report that we have obtained a broken stele, which is an illustration of Daming Palace (small part) and Xingqing Palace (whole). Comparing it with the illustrations drawn in the old chronicles, there are many differences. The illustration has a scale, which is quite precise. The period of the stone carving remains to be verified. We also obtained a Tang Dynasty stele head, stele base, and patterned stele edges, as well as a Tang Dynasty Dugu clan tomb cover, Yihuo coins, Daguan coins, Zhenglong coins, and Song porcelain and Ming Chenghua porcelain fragments. We are still pursuing the main part of Daming Palace, and the work is still in progress. As for the report in the newspaper that both palaces are located outside the Jinhualuo in the eastern suburbs of Xi'an, that is quite a mistake. The palaces in Tang Chang'an City are divided into three places: the West Inner Daji Palace, in the northwest of the current city; the East Inner Daming Palace, in the northeast corner outside the current city; and the South Inner Xingqing Palace, inside and outside the current East Guandong Pass. The current Jinhualuo Village is its eastern boundary. The discovery of the illustrations of the two palaces should be helpful for textual research. According to the report, a broken stele of a part of the Third West Inner Daji Palace was also found next to Xiaoxiangzi Temple Street in the city. With this, the study of the Tang Palace should have new progress.

Baoshan County, this city

Guanlan Compulsory Education Quickly Formulating a Plan 229

Aims to Universalize Education in the County within One Year

And Sets the First Preliminary Announcement Meeting for April 1st

The Baoshan County Education Bureau has spared no effort in experimenting with special education in recent years, such as the Shan-Hai Industrial School and the County-run Xiao Chang two academies. Since their establishment, the results have been very good. Now, in order to universalize education, the county is implementing Guanlan compulsory education, aiming to universalize education in the county within one year, and has set the first preliminary announcement meeting for April 1st. By this day next year, at least 90% of the Baoshan County residents will be able to recognize 1,000 characters, and 95% will be able to sign their own names. The following is an excerpt of its urgent plan:

Principles 230

(1) The people of Baoshan recognize it as their own obligation to strive for universalization, not elite education, not Miss education, not spendthrift education, but voluntary work-study groups. (2) Recognize that society is the school, and integrate the school with society. (3) Recognize that life is education, and integrate life with education. (4) Recognize that the combination of teaching and learning is the most effective way of life, that is, the most effective way of education. Learning and teaching both take doing as the center. (5) Recognize that mental work on labor is the real doing. (6) Recognize that those who know have the obligation to teach others, and those who do not know have the obligation to learn. (7) Recognize that those who know have the obligation to teach others, and those who do not know have the obligation to learn. (7) Recognize that China is a poor country, and Baoshan is a poor county. The poor county in a poor country should use poor methods to universalize the education needed by the poor, and not use wasteful methods to universalize the education not needed by the poor. (8) Recognize that China has reached a critical juncture of life and death, like the Yellow River is about to breach its banks. Even a child who carries a small stone is welcome. Everyone's strength must be called upon to save lives. Every person with knowledge and skills must be called upon to be a teacher or engineer. Every child who has a rudimentary knowledge of writing or is a head of a school must be called upon to be a little teacher or little engineer. (9) Acknowledge that the real education is to enable the public to obtain a kind of combined and promoted power.

Methods 231

(1) Establish a compulsory education college to lay out a compulsory education experiment network, engage in compulsory education research, and serve as the general hub for cultivating engineers in the county. (2) Promulgate an outline for adult work-study groups so that the people of the county can have a basis for automatic progress. Because cotton is the main production in the county, cotton work-study groups should be especially emphasized. The organizational outline should also be promulgated as soon as possible. The 200,000 mu of cotton should have 200 cotton work-study groups. Secondly, horticultural work-study groups are also important. (3) Promulgate an organizational outline for children's work-study groups so that children in various places can proceed automatically. (4) Promulgate procedures for existing schools to convert to work-study groups so that principals and teachers who are interested in converting can have a basis for automatic progress. (5) Issue a notice to all students in the county that they have the obligation to serve as little teachers, and principals and teachers of each school are responsible for guidance and assessment. (6) Issue a notice to schools in cotton-growing areas that each school must assist local cotton farmers in establishing a cotton work-study group and continue to be responsible for guidance. (7) Issue a notice to all literate people in the county to teach two people the characters they know. The obligation to teach people is as important as the obligation to pay taxes. (8) Raise the minimum amount of funding, 15,800 yuan for start-up costs and 35,500 yuan for recurring expenses. (9) Written education should contain compulsion: (A) On April 1, 1934, an order was issued to give a preliminary announcement to the people of the county, limiting them to finish reading the 1,000-character course designated by the county before March 31, 1935, and issuing the second preliminary announcement on June 1. (B) Starting from December 1, 1934, compulsory education will be implemented in the areas covered by the compulsory education experiment network. (C) At the end of December 1935, the universalization of education in the county will be announced. The temporary universalization standard is that 90% of the people above school age can recognize 1,000 characters, and 95% can sign their own names. (D) After the compulsory order is issued, if there are people who are illiterate in the family, shop, factory, or organization without reason, a fine of one yuan per person per month will be imposed according to the number of people, which will be paid by the head of the family, shop owner, factory manager, or organization host. (E) After the compulsory order is issued, literate adults or students who refuse to teach illiterate relatives and friends for whom they are responsible will be fined a dime for refusing to do good deeds and will be announced. (10) In addition to universalizing written education, it is also necessary to universalize production education, science education, self-defense education, transportation education, art education, health education, and relief education. The standards, steps, and deadlines for its universalization will be set separately.

Holding a Magic Competition 237

The first preparatory meeting was specially held in the center at 2:00 pm yesterday. Dozens of magicians, including Jin Chuangfeng, attended. The following methods were adopted: (1) The competition date is set from April 13th to April 17th for five days. The performance time is from 2:00 pm to 5:00 pm every day. It is divided into four groups, each group for 45 minutes. It will be held continuously regardless of whether it is sunny or rainy. (2) All personnel who wish to participate in the competition must fill in the form specified by the center separately and register by April 10th. (3) Participation in the performance, whether as a group or individual, is based on the group as a unit, not on the number of performance programs. (4) The entrance ticket for the audience is set at 2 jiao of foreign currency per ticket, limited to one person. (5) Matters needing attention by the competitors: A. Each competitor should confirm their competition time and must not change it or be absent temporarily. B. Each competitor must arrive at the center 20 minutes before their performance time to prepare. C. The equipment used during the performance must be placed in the place designated by the center. (6) The distribution of ticket sales funds, in addition to the subsidy for the competitors' transportation costs of one yuan per group, is based on three-fifths of the total amount for the purchase of prizes, one-fifth for the expenses of entertaining the judges, and one-fifth for miscellaneous expenses. (7) These methods will be implemented after being passed by the center's affairs meeting.

Commercial News

Finance 240

Silver Case Shelved

Gold Market Rebounds Four Yuan Seventy 241

Short Sellers Disappointed, Rush to Cover Positions

Breaks Through the Sixty Yuan Threshold

After the previous surge in the gold market was dampened, yesterday's silver price saw only a slight increase, bolstering confidence. Simultaneously, favorable news emerged, indicating a continued upward trend. The morning began with overseas silver markets in the UK and US driving the increase. The forward silver price on the Five Metals Exchange rose by only four to half a li, with exchange rates slightly higher. London spot gold fell by four pence, US cotton rebounded by ten points, and US wheat rose by three and seven-five points. Investor sentiment stabilized, and prices rose immediately upon opening. Disappointed short sellers rushed to cover their positions, quickly pushing the price past the sixty yuan threshold. According to the Associated Press, the US Congress has temporarily shelved the silver bill, pending the return of Mr. Rogers from China, with further discussions expected around April 7. Subsequent Reuters reports from Washington indicated that the US Senate has passed a resolution demanding that the Treasury Secretary disclose the list of silver speculators, as the Secretary had previously claimed that those supporting higher silver prices were acting out of self-interest. Simultaneously, news circulated that the government was trying to delay the silver issue, further pushing prices above sixty yuan. Banks became reluctant to buy, and the market fluctuated around sixty yuan, with limited gains and losses, maintaining a stable trend. Money Industry Stipulates Foreign Short-Term Loan Rate 244

|Minimum Not to Fall Below Five Points|

This year, due to the abundance of header linings in the money market and the urgent demand, the market rate for foreign short-term loans has been based on free lending. Recently, rates of two to three points have emerged. However, leaders in the industry, recognizing that daily free lending rates and rates of two to three points were detrimental to the market and observing that the current funds often exceeded demand, without any hope of a turnaround and increase, resolved at the Board of Directors meeting on the 16th of this month to stipulate that from March 21 (i.e., yesterday), the minimum rate for daily foreign short-term loans should be five points, with no subsequent market rate falling below five points. As a result, yesterday's rate was forcibly set at five points, with a strong restriction. The remaining funds of over 3 million were managed by the industry leaders, barely managing to pass. From now on, there will be no more free lending rates or rates of two, three, or four points for foreign short-term loans.

Although it was an abnormal development, it was also caused by human factors. US and UK Cotton Markets are Both Firm and Stable 257

Yesterday, the U.S. cotton market was strong due to the strength of Wall Street and a lack of sellers. Later, it weakened due to some long positions being closed. As a result, spot prices rose by 10 points, and futures prices rose by 9 to 12 points. Liverpool cotton spot prices fell by points, and futures prices rose by 1 point. Egyptian cotton spot prices fell by 10 points. The Bombay cotton market weakened due to long positions being closed, and the closing was quiet. As a result, Pingjar fell by 7.5 jiao, and both Oumra Bai Luo Xi fell by 2.5 rupees. Original telegram records are on the left (telegram of the 20th).
