Food

Spot Flour Market Turns Weak Due to Long Liquidation 259

Yesterday's flour market showed signs of initial stability followed by weakness in all months after the opening. Since the quoted prices for imported wheat fluctuated, with Chicago up by about 2 jiao and Canada down by 1 jiao, the market sentiment was initially stable. Subsequently, long positions were liquidated, and actual sales remained quiet. Therefore, the market sentiment for all months showed signs of loosening, and the sentiment for distant months was even less favorable. When the market opened in the afternoon, prices for all months fell step by step during the third session, down by varying amounts of 1 to 2 fen compared to the morning. Due to small factories selling off and continued long liquidation, the prices for the third session were supported again by long positions in the near-month contract, and large factories still did not resist selling, causing market sentiment to firm up again. However, the prices for all distant months ultimately remained weak and lifeless. As a result, the near-month contract was down by 2.5 li, the April/May contracts were down by 7.5 li, the June contract was down by 2.5 li, the July contract was down by 7.5 li, and the August contract was down by 1.25 fen.

Futures Wheat Market is Stable Near-Term, Weak Distant-Term 260

Yesterday's futures wheat market showed signs of near-term stability and distant-term weakness in all months after the opening in the morning and afternoon. Since the quoted prices for imported wheat were up by about 2 jiao in Chicago and down by 1 jiao in Canada, the near-month contract was still held firm by buyers because delivery was approaching. It was also heard that short sellers were preparing to deliver, and the white wheat had already arrived with the professionals. However, since there were more long positions, the near-term contracts continued to be popular. Seeing that the flour market had softened and the weather would clear up soon after the rain, market sentiment softened for distant-term contracts. As a result, the near-month contract was up by 5 fen, the June contract was down by 1 fen, the July contract was down by 3 fen, and the August contract was down by 1 fen. The spot wheat market saw smooth transactions, and prices remained stable. Kainan Suzhou wheat was at 3 yuan 5 jiao 7 fen, Yingzhou wheat was at 3 yuan 5 jiao 5 fen, Bengbu wheat was at 3 yuan 5 jiao, and Yaowan wheat was at 3 yuan 5 jiao 7 fen, totaling 6,500 bags, which were handled by Fuxin.

Late Rice Market Transactions are Relatively Active 261

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the sources from various gangs were slightly scarcer than before, with only about 30 vendors arriving (over 5,000 shi). However, late rice constituted a large portion, accounting for three-quarters, while thick japonica rice and other varieties only accounted for one-quarter. The sales of late rice were also brisk. Its situation has been quite lively since the beginning of the market, seemingly with an upward trend. Gangs from Northern ports such as Tianjin, Yantai, and Tanggu showed particularly strong interest, competing to purchase. Gangs from Southern ports such as Xiamen and Fuzhou also followed suit. Nearly 3,000 bags of Qingjiao, Song, Si, Feng, Jing, Xi, Lian, and other varieties were traded, and the market price rose slightly by 3 fen. For japonica rice from Chang, Su, Tong, Nangang, and other gangs, the market sentiment was initially firm due to the wind and rain the day before. However, the market turned soft after the weather cleared in the later part of the day. Fortunately, sellers managed to hold the prices firm. Duyang Jian and Yinbian Yuan showed no changes.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, the sources from the river region numbered 22 to 23 vendors. Sales of various varieties in the market remained average. The market for white japonica early thin rice was weak and tired by a few points. High-quality rice from the wharves was scarce and stood firm. The prices of Yang Jian, Du Jian, Ke Jian, and Bai Yuan remained unchanged.

Silk and Tea

New Silkworms About to Hatch, Old Silk Still Abundant 262

Since the beginning of spring, sales of Shandong yellow silk to Europe have almost completely stopped. The Shanghai warehouses have a total of 3,825 boxes of Shandong yellow coarse silk and yellow factory silk in stock. With the new spring cocoons about to enter the market, silk merchants lack funds to purchase cocoons. They are currently petitioning the Shandong provincial government to issue 500,000 yuan in silk public bonds to rescue the silk industry.

The production of Shanghai Shuang Gong silk is decreasing day by day, while the demand from India remains. The existing inventory is about to be sold out. In recent days, only 15 packages of Shuang Gong silk were exported to India on British ships. Overseas raw silk prices remain unstable. Japanese silk is being sold aggressively without letup, and there are no signs of changes in the silk telegrams from Europe and the United States. Shanghai merchants also have no silk telegrams to send out. Foreign firms are unmoved, and silk merchants are also taking a wait-and-see attitude. The market atmosphere is tired and quiet. Spring silkworms in Zhejiang are emerging, and Shanghai mills have abundant silk in stock. The future is increasingly pessimistic.

The Number of Pingshui Tea Firms Has Increased Significantly 263

Due to weak sales to the United States last year, many Pingshui green tea manufacturers in Shaoxing, Zhejiang, switched to producing tea for export to French firms, which yielded a small profit. As a result, tea merchants are unusually enthusiastic about the tea industry in that region this year. The number of tea firms has increased from over 50 to 80 or 90, and the situation is quite active.

There is Over-Supply of Metal Rebar 264

Currently, the inventory of rebar is exceptionally high, and there are even more arrivals. Therefore, the market is largely oversupplied. Standard prices have been quietly declining, estimated at 107 yuan per ton, down another yuan from before. It is heard that, aside from sporadic purchases from construction gangs, there have been very few large-scale transactions in recent days.

Spring and Autumn

The Ancients Are Not As Good As People Today 279

— Yan Qiao

Speaking of art, people today may not be inferior to the ancients, but generally people always [value the ancient and despise the present]. Remember Bai Letian's letter to Yuan Weizhi, which said, [Honoring the past and despising the present is a great human emotion]. No one has ever dared to belittle the ancients. Please read Tian Wen's Collection of Ancient Joy Hall, which says; [I observe that the ancient people's broken slips and residual pens, remaining ink and scraps of paper, all have excellent points. Writing is not only in Han Yu and Liu Zongyuan, poetry is not only Li Bai, Du Fu, Wang Wei, and Meng Haoran, calligraphy is not only Ouyang Xun, Yu Shinan, Chu Suiliang, and Xue Ji, painting is not only in Gu Kaizhi, Lu Tanwei, Zhang Sengyou, Wu Daozi, Jing Hao, Guan Tong, Dong Yuan, and Ju Ran. The same is true of utensils, not only are recent ancient times not as good as distant ancient times, but even ten years ago is better than ten years later by a factor of ten, a hundred, or a thousand. Why is the world declining?] This is an absolute pro-ancient faction.

Since the rise of the Restoration, the ancients have been overthrown, and everyone has uttered a [modern] word. At best, everything before this day and this time already belongs to the outdated. This kind of reaction can be considered the most rigid and strongest. However, after quietly observing society, I feel that this reaction is still unreliable. The same new reaction has occurred, and people seem to be [expressing their nostalgic thoughts and expressing their ancient sentiments]. This is an undeniable fact, and there are examples everywhere.

In my opinion, in terms of artistic technique, there is no need to be modest. The ancients were indeed inferior to people today. Just talking about riddles, like [Yellow silk young wife grandson, White,] hiding [Exquisite words], how clumsy! Later riddle-makers really fought wits and entered a state of divine transformation, which the ancients could never have imagined. No wonder Pan Zuyin thought of [My eastern neighbor has a virgin, and those who spy on me have been doing so for three years], guessing the Tang poem [It's always the feelings of Yumen Pass]. He wanted to offer a heavy reward of a hundred gold. In terms of the spirit of art, it seems that the works of the ancients are more profound and dignified than those of today, what is called [ancient and fragrant]. This is also rooted in the psychology of respecting the ancients, and cannot be said to be just a matter of the times.

I have a seal engraved with [Do not despise modern people and love the ancients], which seems to be a line of poetry. The poet who made this line of poetry has a good mind and attitude. His words "do not despise" have already broken the traditional concept of respecting the ancients, and have other ideas. But he can reconcile extremes, hold on to both sides, and use them in the middle. Not bad! This is also the mind and attitude that we artists should have.

The Philosophy of Buying Aviation Lottery Tickets 280

— Ding Ming

The National Government is holding lottery tickets for the construction of aviation highways, and this is the fifth time!

In the past four times, all those who bought them must have been like the full moon on the fifteenth day of the eighth lunar month, happy for those who were happy and sad for those who were sad; and this time to the future ten thousand times, why would it be any different?

But today I am telling people who buy aviation lottery tickets with infinite joy and happiness; it is important to hold on to [the philosophy of buying aviation lottery tickets].

What I call the philosophy of aviation lottery tickets is nothing more than the following two principles;

(1) If you win this time, continue to come again next time; if you don't win this time, you must work harder next time.

(2) Winning the prize is a success; if you are happy not to become a public figure, you are also happy.

Look at that drop of water, it has a source and a destination; a discarded chess piece has a process of generation and a destination to drift away.

Just like the Yangtze River and the Yellow River, mighty and mighty, converging countless streams, flowing eastward into the sea; the sea also merges with the Pacific Ocean; the sun evaporates, turns into steam and forms clouds, drips rain, and becomes streams again, and rushes into the rivers, circulating and flowing, forming the main land system of the Eastern Hemisphere, and forming the entire cosmic spectacle. The changes never end. The spectacle never ends.

The life and death of human beings, and all states of things, are exactly like this; since there is you as a living being in the world, it is very natural that there will be an end to your life. All kinds of things, let them be natural, and treat yourself like water; especially the earth-shattering money craze, buying aviation lottery tickets!

Even if you can't really get your wish, you can still proudly boast and tell people; [I have donated several yuan to the aviation highway construction fund! ······ It's nothing more than being enthusiastic and fulfilling the obligations of a citizen! ] Or take out the used tickets and give them to friends and relatives, saying; [I bought this for you! ···· You got zero points, you have no money! ······ ]

In any case, in yourself, you can say; [I won the first prize! ]

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 282

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 26

Generously Explaining His Mind, Forgetting His Family and Serving the Country, Jiang Liang Faces the Jade Mirror and Sighs for My Lost One

The four company commanders stood up tall, answering in unison with a "can" word. Bao Fang brought a few smiles, nodding his head and saying; That's good. I also said the same, there are no rubber men who work with my Bao Fang, all thumbs up. But then again, only we know this great truth, the brothers can't understand it, you have to explain this meaning to him well. Today, haven't the planes come yet? Speaking, he smiled faintly, and then said; It doesn't matter, I have already calculated this move. But you have to go and tell the brothers well, don't panic, you should take this matter lightly, Yin Daren smiled and said; We naturally know this. Bao Fang was very happy to see that the four company commanders were of one heart and helping himself. He also talked to them in detail for a while before letting them go. Zhao Ziqiang returned to the company headquarters, still full of ambition, feeling that since he was a soldier, he had to fight for a breath for the Chinese people. People live to be a hundred years old, and they still die, what is life, and besides, I have been on the front line several times, and I am still alive, so fighting is not necessarily dangerous. If we win two battles with our people and earn some reputation for the Northeast Army, then it would be a matter of both fame and fortune, he thought casually, and unknowingly lay down on that big earthen bed. But when his head was raised, he was facing the yellow earthen wall, and the red paper couplets pasted on the wall, shot into his eyes, and then he remembered the joyous couplets in his own home, and along with that he also thought of his beloved wife, Guizhi. I have inspired patriotism here, preparing to sacrifice myself, what if there is a little danger, what will she do? She would lose her husband after only five days of marriage. It was too tragic. He remembered that when she was sent to the long-distance bus station, her face was covered with tears, but with a smile. How uncomfortable she was in her heart. He married such a beautiful wife, but he could not enjoy it himself. This life is in vain. (342)

Another Method for Treating Goldfish with White Spot Disease 283

— Chen Canyu

After reading Mr. Wu Jiren's [A Tale of Protecting Goldfish in Cold Weather] in this publication, I deeply admire his rich experience in raising fish. However, electrotherapy is difficult for treating white spots on the body of the fish, and ink treatment is also inconvenient. Here is a simple and effective method, recorded as follows, for adoption by fellow enthusiasts.

In the hot summer, take several pieces of mud brick, immerse them in a urine pit, and after three days, take them out and dry them, then soak them again, and dry them again. Repeat this four or five times, until the color of the brick fully absorbs the urine and turns black; then dry it extremely well and store it in the room, waiting for the warm spring, to put it at the bottom of the tank. In warm weather, the fish's body is almost always rubbing against the top or bottom of the tank due to illness, so putting this brick can make it rub against it; then the fish's body will no longer develop mold spots, and even if mold has already grown, it can be eliminated immediately after rubbing. I have raised fish for more than ten years, and since I obtained this method, the lively golden scales of the gods have no more fear of dying from mold. According to ancient methods of raising fish, all used yellow sand pit tanks that had been stored with manure, and those with piled pit sand were considered the best; the idea is to take its full saline content, which is beneficial to the health of the fish's body?

Furthermore, to prevent severe cold and freezing, a wooden tank cover can be used to cover the mouth of the tank, and then rice straw can be used as a mat and covered on the lid; so that the grass will not scatter on the surface of the water, and the gaps in the wooden lid will still allow air to circulate. The body of the tank is further wrapped in layers of this straw mat, which can be removed after spring. If this can be done, then the tank water is guaranteed not to freeze. Because Mr. Wu's method is not perfect, it is attached here.

Everything is a Deception? 284

— Yan Chonglou

Recently, a film star, disheartened, committed suicide. In her last moments, she said, "Everything is a deception!"

"Deception" is the enemy of "honesty." It is a vast chasm that hinders human evolution and the cause of countless evils in the world.

I myself once said, "People are deceived when they are young, and when they grow up, they deceive others." But I eventually felt that my words were too generalized! And the saying "everything is a deception" is also too much! Although in this transitional era, "deception" has become a prevalent social malady, we cannot, because deception is prevalent, conclude that there is no truth in the universe. At the very least, one cannot admit to oneself that one is a deception. Such a subjective mentality is enough to create tragedies like the suicide of that film star.

Great creation! Supreme maternal love! Passionate friendship! ...... Can you say that these are all deceptions? We must believe that everything in the world is real, and deception is just a fleeting bubble, although there are indeed many people living by trickery in the present world.

However, the pathological development of deception and the decline of the capitalist system are directly proportional; therefore, the issue of deception is also a serious problem in society today.

Pilgrimage to Europe 285

— Zhang Ruogu

(IV) The Carnival of Nice

The people of the French provinces love outdoor life. When various folk or religious festivals arrive, they often hold various games, processions, and competitions in the streets and squares. In the past, during religious pilgrimages, there were often many believers wearing various colors of penitential robes. [This was a coarse cloth gown without sleeves, with a cowl-like hat hanging on the back, covering the head and only revealing the face. Today, monks in monastic orders still wear this type of penitential robe, such as former Chinese Prime Minister Lu Zhengxiang, who often wears it now.] This has not yet disappeared. In various concerts preserving folk customs and music, we can still often see various ancient inherited musical instruments.

Many cities and villages still hold various bizarre festivals every year, such as the "Monster Model Image" in Tarascon (in southern France, during the Saint Martha's festival, there are often performances of various monsters and beasts in the marching pageants), the Brahman-style procession of Saint Mary's, the ceremony of celebrating the sea, and the "Telling Tall Tales" in Saint-Tropez, etc., all of which are extremely interesting contest decorations.

But among all the festivals held in the southern French provinces, the most wonderful and exciting is the "Carnival" of Nice.

The term "Carnival" is a transliteration of the French word "Carnaval" and refers to a period of revelry. Originally, it was a day for worshiping the god of wine. This festival usually takes place a few days before the Catholic Lent, so some people translate it as "Meat Festival" or "Mardi Gras". On this day, according to customs in various parts of Europe, everyone can eat, drink, shout, make noise, dance, and frolic to their heart's content. The "Carnival" festivals in Venice, Italy, and Nice, France, are famous worldwide.

Many people who love to seek pleasure mostly rush to Nice in early February, specifically to participate in the annual "Carnival." It has the same meaning as people from the provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang in China going to Hangzhou to catch the "Incense Tide".

In Nice, the Carnival is jointly prepared and organized by the local city hall and the municipal committee. The purpose is to attract wealthy foreign tourists to visit Nice, so that the market can prosper.

The people of France originally have a character that loves to seek pleasure, and they often like to seize the opportunity of holidays to desperately seek happiness. When they arrive at the "Carnival" festival, they want to play and seek happiness more than ever. Because this is a day of unrestrained eating and drinking, the streets and shops are decorated with colorful colors during the day, and at night, the lights are lit up, shining like daylight. They organize various strange-shaped parades, singing and walking around the streets. You can dance on the road, you can throw flowers at women, you can dress up and disguise as various characters, wear strange and ridiculous costumes, and run around wildly, stopping unfamiliar women to dance wildly. Adults have become naughty children, specializing in teasing and joking with others, or throwing flowers at each other, or dragging beautiful women from vehicles to hug and kiss. Because everyone wears masks, they cannot recognize each other's true faces. During this season, many infatuated men and resentful women get married because of this, which is a common occurrence.

The best-looking thing is all kinds of strange and bizarre masquerade floats. In the 1933 parade, there were many strange masquerade characters. For example, on a camel-shaped car, a snake-head ring was hung high on the camel's hump, and a young man in sports shorts sat in the center, accompanied by a girl decorated as a princess holding a large feather fan. On a horse-head boat, a pot-bellied Parisian male god hugged a petite Helen goddess. A singing cicada was begging a stingy ant for dry food. A monkey king was drooling as he looked at the cattle, sheep, chickens, and pigs under his seat. A bald head and a big nose were covered with many mosquitoes. (Probably a philosopher) A long-haired and long-bearded musician was riding on a three-mouthed bird and dancing wildly while conducting.

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly Shanghai Chamber of Commerce National Goods Mall Special Issue

A Word for the National Goods Industry and Those Who Use National Goods 286

— Wang Xiaolai

When we see the statistics on imports and exports for January, the trade deficit reaches 40,960,729 yuan, which is greater than the trade deficit statistics for the fourth year of the Republic of China. Everyone will say in unison, "This is terrible!" In President Roosevelt's recovery plan, cash will be absorbed and silver prices will be raised. Our country's survey of silver bars stored in this city shows that two-thirds are held by foreigners. Everyone will be even more shocked and say, "This is terrible!" After the Shanghai Ceasefire Agreement, foreign goods were dumped and enemy goods were even more popular. Their movements were like mercury spilling on the ground, infiltrating everywhere, even in remote villages and mountainous areas. And the general unenterprising elements are greedy for cheapness, quenching thirst with poison, or dislike national goods for being inferior, preferring to buy foreign goods, thinking they are beautiful, and there are even those who only use foreign goods. Speaking of this, everyone will say even more, "This is terrible, unenterprising things, shameless traitors!" Those foreigners are really scary! If we talk about my country's agriculture, which has a long history and is recognized by the world, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce released grain import statistics for the 22nd year, with a total value of 274,303,434 yuan last month. According to reports, the freight obtained by various countries in China due to shipping last year was statistically 2,149,880,983 taels. Everyone listens and is dumbfounded, saying that if this continues, it will be really "terrible!" In addition, the silk industry has plummeted, the national goods market is declining, and internal wars are frequent, the communist bandits are rampant, the borders are shrinking day by day, and foreign insults are increasing. Everyone is urgently shouting, "This is terrible!" "This is terrible!" Really "terrible!" What does this one hundred and twenty "terrible" and one hundred and eight thousand "terrible" mean? Is it more powerful than three thousand planes and forty tons of poison gas?

Try to analyze the meaning of these three words "This is terrible", which contain infinite sadness, one hundred and twenty unwillingness, and are trapped in helplessness. In other words, it is a manifestation of following old ways and drifting along, being at the mercy of others. But when we think of the glory of the nation's future, and to strive for self-improvement, who is willing to mislead themselves and be ridiculed for a five-minute craze, and for the Eastern Sleeping Lion not to awaken? Our country has vast land, abundant resources, and a large population, and is famous in the world. Heroes have a place to use their skills, and the future is always bright. National steps can always be promoted! The national spirit can always be promoted! It's just that if we always say "This is terrible", then there is really nothing we can do. Some people say that the British do it first and then talk about it; the Germans only do it and don't talk about it; the French ...... the Chinese talk about it and don't do it, which is a true portrayal of the three words "This is terrible". Therefore, from now on, as long as we work hard and forge ahead, we are not afraid of hardships, we are not afraid of the trend, and regardless of everything, we start from individual practical actions and practical struggles, then we will have a savior.

We merchants, in this era of commercial warfare, our position is so important, our qualifications are so noble, and the time to strive for progress cannot be delayed any longer. Those who call themselves members of the national goods industry are even more leaders in commerce. "The days are passing," "The years do not wait for me," the sales channels for foreign goods are ultimately within the scope of our national territory. I still remember reading in the newspaper the other day that the Japanese, due to the world's active boycott of goods, have declared to the League of Nations that they will withdraw from the tariff truce to show their retaliation. With their qualifications as an advanced country, how patriotic are the Japanese people, and they are still actively carrying out this plan. What about our country? We don't want to dump national goods into foreign markets, and we can't even do the minimum of selling our own goods to ourselves. How ashamed are we? Are we even worthy of being called Chinese citizens? Therefore, our association established a commodity exhibition hall in the tenth year of the Republic of China; later, we held national goods exhibitions and temporary national goods malls, a total of seven times. In recent years, we have also exhibited national goods in Hangzhou, Qingdao, Weihaiwei, Zhenjiang, Ningbo, Bengbu, Jinan, Hankou and other places to promote national attention and awakening. In June of the twentieth year of the Republic of China, we opened the national goods mall on the lower floor of the commodity exhibition hall on North Henan Road in this city. Yesterday, the national goods mall in Nanshi also opened. We are very supportive of the China National Goods Company and the Shanghai National Goods Company on Nanjing Road, as well as other merchants and factories in this and other places that specialize in selling and manufacturing national goods, because the more of these malls, the better. They are the lifeline of our country, so we must value them. As for the efforts of our association, it is nothing more than being forced by the demands of the times. As the saying goes, "The tiger is already at our heels, we really don't have time to see if it's male or female." However, although this is the case, our association is a group of merchants, and we only have the instinct to promote national goods, and we have very few opportunities to study them, and we don't have the strength to produce them. In practice, we rely entirely on our merchants, factories, and compatriots who use national goods. All the past things are like yesterday's death; all the future things are like today's birth. Everyone works together, moves forward, and no matter how foreign goods are dumped, how beautiful they are, how convenient and durable they are, I only use my national goods! Merchants and factories must, on the one hand, take into account the purchasing power of customers; on the other hand, they must carefully study how to make their products excellent and fast; on the one hand, even if they are subject to various encroachments of foreign goods, they must exhaust their efforts and use all their strength to find a way out of death. With such a two-pronged approach, our national goods will have a turning point, and the national situation can develop, and "terrible" things will naturally gradually decrease, until they disappear.

This year is the Year of Women's National Goods, which happens to be the auspicious period for the birth of our association's Nanshi National Goods Mall. I would like to express my sincere wishes to my compatriots in the national goods industry and to the compatriots who use national goods for unlimited progress!

The Past and Future of National Goods Malls 287

— Wang Yansong

Ever since the opening of the sea, foreign insults have become increasingly urgent. People of insight have realized that the economic aggression of imperialism is more serious than politics. So they rose up to advocate the boycott of goods movement. However, since the fourth year of the Republic of China, there have been more than ten boycotts of goods in total. However, foreign goods still fill the market as before. The customs trade deficit has also increased year by year. I know that the boycott of goods is not enough to be effective. So they rose up to promote national goods. The national goods mall came into being accordingly. And it is the backbone of promoting national goods.

The existence of the national goods mall in Shanghai dates back to ten years ago. At that time, there was a national goods market in Nanshi. And the original site of Mayushan Company on Nanjing Road also had the establishment of a national goods mall. Ultimately, due to poor organization. They all disappeared after a flash. Foreign goods further used their dumping policy. Flowing freely within the country. As a result, wealth is exhausted. The people are increasingly trapped. National goods are becoming increasingly decadent. In view of this, our association, in the twentieth year of the Republic of China, demarcated a site in the commodity exhibition hall north of Tianhou Palace. Established a national goods mall. Painstaking management. Extensive publicity. Thus aroused the public's psychology of loving and using national goods. And the sales channels of national goods. Gradually developed. National goods markets. Also emerged one after another. Now our association has established a second national goods mall at the original site of the County Chamber of Commerce in front of Xiaonanmen in Nanshi. I believe that at this time of the Women's National Goods Year. And national goods malls. Springing up one after another like mushrooms after rain. It is a good phenomenon in the national goods industry.

Although. This is only in Shanghai. However, the dumping of foreign goods. Deep into the interior. National goods malls in the interior. There are also some established. But there are not many. Languid. As a result, the customs trade deficit. Still as before. But recently, the national goods movement in the interior. The cooperative movement. Advocacy is quite laborious. Therefore, the future of national goods malls. It will certainly reach the interior. From cities to townships. From ordinary malls. And become cooperative stores. If you don't believe me. You can wait and see.

Overview of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce National Goods Mall 288

— Hui

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce National Goods Mall. Founded on June 6th of the twentieth year of the Republic of China, it is located in the commodity exhibition hall building north of Tianhou Palace Bridge. Initially, there was only one floor of shop space. The following year, it was expanded into two floors. This year, the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs moved to the city center. The original site of the former County Chamber of Commerce was vacated. After a regular meeting, it was decided. That is, to establish a second mall. Named Nanshi National Goods Mall. Its organizational situation. And the size of the area. It is roughly the same as the first mall in the north of the city. As a result, the two malls are divided between the north and south. The supply of national goods to the whole city. It is more convenient. Examining the association's national goods sales agency. Its history dates back more than ten years. The initial commodity exhibition hall opened on November 1st of the tenth year of the Republic of China. At the same time, the first exhibition was held. A collection of products from all over the country. Displayed in one hall. It is a pioneering initiative in Shanghai. Chinese and foreign people. Upon visiting the institute. They all praised the progress of Chinese craftsmanship. Frequently ask to buy. Afterwards, there are more and more special letters and inquiries. However, the exhibits of the commodity exhibition hall. All are long-term displays. Anyone can visit. It seems that it cannot be used for visitors to choose and buy at will. In order to promote the sales channels of the producers. And for the convenience of buyers of high-quality national goods. In July of the eleventh year of the Republic of China. After deliberation by the Commodity Exhibition Hall Committee. Established a sales department. And designate the lower central part of the exhibition hall. As a place of business. That is, on October 6th of this year. It opened simultaneously with the silk exhibition. Major national goods manufacturers in this and other places. There are more than one hundred companies that send products to the association and request to sell them on their behalf. However, due to insufficient publicity. And lack of shop space. Business has not been fully developed. But since the establishment. For many years. Have achieved considerable results. In between

From the fourteenth to the seventeenth year of the Republic of China. When the National Goods Exhibition is held every year. There is also a temporary national goods mall attached. Each session lasts about one month. The amount of business. Ultimately reached hundreds of thousands of yuan. In the twentieth year of the Republic of China. After the city chamber of commerce's regular meeting. The original sales department of the commodity exhibition hall will be closed. Changed to National Goods Mall. Take the entire lower level as the place of business. Attract major national goods manufacturers. Set up counters to sell high-quality products. Perfect organization. Extensive publicity. That is, it opened on June 6th of this year. The entire market is divided into more than twenty departments. Collect all kinds of goods. Reached thousands of kinds. The business is very prosperous. The following year. The commodity exhibition hall building was expanded to four floors. Expanded the mall to two floors. (The third and fourth floors are still exhibition halls.) The location is getting bigger. The more goods it can hold. And the business is becoming more and more developed. On March 21st of this year. The Nanshi National Goods Mall also opened. The organization is more perfect. Therefore, the situation at the beginning. Record it for reference for those who care about national goods.

China's Secret Suicide 289

— Yinge

The relationship between silver prices and national goods is very close. In other words, the silver price is the opposite of the currency price of each country. If the silver price is high, the foreign currency is cheap. If the foreign currency is cheap, the foreign goods are cheap. Foreign goods are cheap and easy to sell to China, which is called dumping. Like seawater pouring over. 700 million in the 22nd year of the Republic of China, 700 million again in the 23rd year, and again in the 24th year... No matter if it is the Year of Men's National Goods or the Year of Women's National Goods, dumping and more dumping, the entire China will have no life. This disaster. People who are not very careful about the economy may not fully feel its harm. In fact, its severity is even above the Northeast issue. Now all countries are engaged in dumping, of course, the United Kingdom, the United States, and Russia are not polite. Among them, the most outstanding is Japan. Alas, Japan is the enemy. Japanese goods are enemy goods. Why do your noble countrymen welcome everything from staple cotton yarn and white sugar to children's goods? Needless to say, it is because Japanese goods are cheap. You think, why can Japanese goods be cheap? This is of course because the Japanese yen has fallen in price. The reason for the price drop is of course because of their suspension of exchange policy. However, it is still the Chinese who fall into his trap and help the tyrant. Since the Seiyukai cabinet suspended the exchange of the yen, although the market price of Japanese exchange has not been seen in ordinary Japanese altars in Shanghai for a long time. However, foreign banks, especially Japanese banks, are doing business as usual. (This cannot blame foreigners) When rich Chinese people are in this year of economic depression, all kinds of businesses feel that it is not easy to make profits. When they see that the Japanese yen has suspended exchange, they know that it will definitely fall in price, so everyone sends money to foreign banks. Throw out the Japanese yen. This huge amount of money, directly and indirectly, will reach the hands of the Japanese. Since Chinese businessmen throw out the yen together, its price will definitely be suppressed, the more they throw out, the more suppressed. As a result, the yen has fallen sharply, and all Japanese goods are very cheap. This is clearly using Chinese capital to help Japan's dumping. This is called secret suicide.

Dedicated to the Women of the [Women's National Products Year] 293

— Wu Yafei

The National Products Year has passed, but I dare not say anything about the past year. However, regarding the approaching [Women's National Products Year], I can’t help but utter a few words. Because the reality is before my eyes, forcing me to speak!

Before I unfold the main text, I must first look back at the achievements of last year's [National Products Year]. Those who sell enemy goods still sell them in large quantities, willing to betray their conscience and act as unscrupulous merchants. What can be done about it! Those who love to use imported or enemy goods do not seem to have their patriotism aroused by the call for [National Products Year] or change their attitude. The most hateful are those shameless merchants who blatantly disguise enemy goods and pass them off as national products for sale! It's truly reached the extreme of madness. I don't know where their conscience is, where their personality exists? In the past, there was the line in Tang poetry, [Merchant girls do not know the sorrow of national subjugation], but now I want to change it to [Merchants do not know the sorrow of national subjugation]. If you go to the Jianghai Customs to check the statistics of imported foreign goods, I believe the import amount for 1933 will definitely not be less than in previous years.

Not long ago, according to the guidance office of the International Trade Bureau, from January to September 1933, the import of foreign wines and cigarettes reached a weak ten million gold yuan. The import of rouge, perfume, and other cosmetics amounted to 1,396,684 yuan, with French goods accounting for the majority, followed by Japanese and American goods. Seeing the above two statistics of consumables, I was speechless. Our upper-class Chinese, young masters, young ladies, and mistresses, are ultimately quite extravagant. Although they are in a situation of internal and external troubles, natural disasters and man-made disasters, their indulgence in luxury remains unchanged. Those above the middle class are not short of people who live extravagantly. One garment costs a hundred gold, and one meal costs ten gold. It still cannot be called extravagant. It is necessary to pursue extreme luxury, with foreign goods being the only way to show off. Therefore, the import of foreign consumables has increased year by year. [A rich man's dinner is half a year's food for a poor family], who can deny it?

This year is [Women's National Products Year]. Then, I should ask those wives, mistresses, and young ladies to change their attitude of loving foreign goods and disliking national products, and to promote national products as much as possible! Last year's [National Products Year] was like this, let's see about [Women's National Products Year]!

Some people advocate that promoting national products should start with women first, which shows the importance of women's relationship with national products. Women are the mothers of the nation. I respectfully offer a sincere heart here to wish the women of the [Women's National Products Year] to fulfill their responsibility of promoting national products based on their natural duty as the mothers of the nation, and not just pursue fashion while abandoning the mission they should bear.

National Products Road and National Products Week 294

— Qian Zuizhu

Doing things under the slogan [The revolution has not yet succeeded] naturally requires some revolutionary spirit; moreover, who can refute the promotion of the National Products Year.

Based on this principle, to promote national products, one should work with a decisive spirit. [Meetings], [posting slogans], [exhibitions], [big sales] have already shown that [it is not very effective]. This [road to failure] does not seem to need to be taken again. To wake up from the dream and change the situation, one must find another [way out].

In my stupid mind, I have thought of several methods. Although they seem a bit radical, good medicine tastes bitter, and when you first take it, it certainly won't taste as good as [candied arsenic]. I hastily and disrespectfully write them below:

(1) National Products Week: The central government is the head of the whole country, and its influence is most likely to achieve the effect of [changing customs and habits]. Therefore, I request that when holding [Commemorative Weeks], it be stipulated that all attendees must wear national products. (I have never shown my face at weekly meetings, and I don't know if the clothing is uniform? In principle, for the sake of solemnity, such venues should comply with regulations and attend in national formal attire, | | blue robe and black mandarin jacket | | is the right thing to do. Beforehand, people should be assigned to check at the check-in point. If they are wearing foreign goods, they will not be allowed to attend. The staff, fearing the punishment of not attending, will of course quickly change their ways.

At the same time, the central party headquarters seems to be able to do the same, because it is the highest authority leading the people. As long as these two gatherings are tentatively renamed [National Products Week] during this year's [Commemorative Week], I think it will definitely have a great impact.

(2) National Products Road: In cities where foreign forces cannot interfere (or start from the capital), choose a prosperous street and designate it as [National Products Road]. At both ends of this road, national product promotion organizations should send people daily, together with the police, to pay attention to observing pedestrians. If there are people wearing foreign goods from head to toe, flaunting them in the market, they will be refused to walk on the National Products Road. (Those who disobey orders will be punished according to the regulations for violating police orders.)

Shops selling foreign goods on National Products Road are only allowed to close, not open. It is hoped that they will be gradually eliminated, so as to achieve the goal of National Products Road exclusively selling national products.

Enough, enough, don't have too many methods, just do it. If someone agrees, I can write in more detail and discuss it with everyone.

Doing this not only shows the government's genuine spirit of promoting national products, but also shows the people's determination to work together to save the country. If this minimum requirement cannot be met, and the easiest work to implement is not willing to be done, then there is no need to say anything else that sounds good.

Women? The situation is urgent! The country is in danger! Don't yearn for the fashion of using foreign goods anymore, and fall into the dangerous situation of bankruptcy.

New Force 297

— Shi Qi

Buddhism seems to be very popular lately. In the past forty or fifty years, people's livelihoods and national plans have been turned upside down, and ordinary people are probably a bit troubled, exhausted, and feel that it is not like the world anymore. Then, seeking peace, seeking complete enlightenment, seeking to return to one's original face, is exactly this time. Drawing clear springs from the source of a fresh religion to quench spiritual thirst, like travelers in the desert, can roughly explain this reason!

Thinking back to before and after the Russian Revolution, there were always passionate dreams and the sorrow of disillusionment. After each failure, many reformers fled, suffered, and turned into nihilists, pursuing sexual desire, like the character of Sanin written by Artzybashev. However, the emotions of our Eastern nations are slightly different. Once they have failed or are oppressed to the point of barely being able to live, the only escape and comfort is to take refuge in the Three Jewels, or become a lay Buddhist, gradually entrusting their spirit to another world, isolating themselves from the present world. There are countless such figures in history.

But what distinguishes Buddhism from other religions is that it is all-encompassing and includes everything. For example, the eight negations of the Middle Treatise and the two emptinesses of the Only Consciousness theory, when it comes to the result, there is no law and no being, and all appearances are illusions. Then what do people do in the world, why don't they die? Neither born nor dead, neither alive nor dead, there is no so-called life and death.

We must absolutely not ignore this great force, which can be used to reform society, transcending life and death to achieve great courage and fearlessness, becoming a fighter for light, an eliminator of darkness, and a builder of a new society. Faith and reason unite to become a great force, strong yet peaceful, sweeping away everything, destroying everything, and building everything!

Seclusion 298

— Zang Kejia

I have decided to move.

It's like undertaking a revolutionary undertaking, decided after several hesitations. Knowing clearly that this action cannot be understood by ordinary people, I don't want to make things too strange, so I confessed to others:

[I'm going to move.]

After saying this sentence, I didn't wait for people to ask the reason and continued. I said that I can't sleep well at night in the school, and my heart is like being clamped in an iron plate, being oppressed. I really feel funny myself, no matter what I say, can people not allow it? Moreover, my mental disorder has long been registered in everyone's mind. I told them the address of my new home, but the situation of the room is for them to discover themselves. Now it's time to say something about the new home. It's a relative's outbuilding not far from the school. I also spent a lot of effort to live in this small house. They didn't let me live in it, saying that this small house was too undignified for my status, and they were afraid that others would criticize them for treating guests poorly, but I finally lived here.

A room leaning against the east wall, with mountains outside the wall. The room is so small that stretching out your arms can connect the north and south walls. A few bed boards are placed against the east wall, and a small table occupies a small gap under the east wall. There are no windows, nothing else. When entering the door, you have to be careful of your head, and you have to be careful that the door pushes you back, because a corner of the small table prevents it from being fully opened. It is said that it should be very pleasant to be in a high-rise building, leaning on a deck chair, sipping tea and watching the sea, or chatting with a few people, but I moved down from this high-rise building. I am happy like this. Under the sun, I feel suffocated. In this way, after class, returning to this small resting place, everything will be calm. Closing the small door tightly, not seeing anything, at this time, I become a free person.

Every morning I get up early and run to school, just bypassing some mountains and forests, and then run back in the evening. I feel a deep interest inside, suppressing the darkness in my heart and forcing myself to say:

[A young student].

Sharing the bed is a worker. We are about the same age. From his foolish smile, I found the deepest comfort. He likes to sing, but it can't really be called singing. I asked him:

[What's the appeal of singing opera?]

[The appeal is great... I can't say it... It's better than getting married!] Sometimes he also recites poetry. Once he recited...

[During the Qingming season, it rains endlessly, the travelers on the road are heartbroken...]

[What does this rain sentence mean?] I asked him.

[What does it mean? When it rains, the road is difficult to walk, and the travelers are worried.]

He said he had studied in a private school for eight years. He laughed at me for reading Mao Shi and Zuo Zhuan... He said he had read these books long ago, but now he doesn't know anything.

I remember the first night I moved in, the little aunts and sisters came to congratulate me on my new home with flowers and tea. They said very tactfully, this is the first night, and we won't bother you in the future.

The next day, someone came to see me, but couldn't find me. It turned out that my small house was covered by the high-rise building. When he got to the room, he first patrolled everywhere with his eyes, and finally said... [It's very interesting, it would be better if there was a window].

As usual, I couldn't sleep well at night. A pair of eyes turned frantically. Fortunately, this is at night (when is it not at night?) On my own bed, my thoughts can be freely up and down, underground and then above the sky.

[Haven't you been to the front line?] Someone is asking.

[Yes; I am sick now. But my heart is not dead!]

Answering, I remembered Yinri again.

My Confession 299

— He Jiahai

After Zhuan Peng published his confession, I had a very serious reflection, and my friends also had very severe criticisms of me. Although I understood the causes and circumstances before and after this incident and the intentions of those [righteous] gentlemen, from my own standpoint, what I should do at this time is to mercilessly dissect my past behavior, and very honestly judge myself before embarking on a solid new path. As a result of this self-reflection, I feel that there is still a need to speak again.

First of all, I must state that my attitude when I wrote that article [About My Creation] last time was not sincere, just like many of my past behaviors were not honest. To make the facts clearer, I will now very frankly and sincerely explain to the readers.

When I heard the news that my novels were all written by Xu Jun, I asked him if he had spread it himself, but he strongly denied it:

[There is no such thing, absolutely no such thing. If this matter is publicized, it will not only be harmful to you, but also to me, because people will say that we are colluding with each other.]

Just like believing in myself, I believed that his words were reliable. But soon our friend Peng Chenghui told me that Zhuan Peng had seen a message about me posted in Cultural Train by a certain gentleman, which was very unfavorable to me, and if it was published, he would be very sorry for me. At this time, I began to realize that so-called friends are like this. But I didn't say anything. A few days later, I received a letter from Zhuan Peng from Hangzhou:

[Many guys are jealous of you and like to make trouble, and things have finally stirred up. Yesterday I saw Ba Jin, and Ba Jin also asked about it. Because of this matter, I have been uneasy for several days, and I have also discussed it with Chenghui, Zhenliang and other friends, but there is no good strategy. I have been friends with you for six or seven years, like brothers, but this matter seems inconvenient to talk about in person, for fear of making you angry. Your ability to do things is above mine, I hope you can find a way to quell this storm...]

I got this letter and felt very funny. After seeing Mr. Shi Heng's article and finding out that Qingdaofu was the pseudonym of that gentleman, I realized that the occurrence of this incident was not accidental, but a planned coercion towards me; at the same time, I also understood why Zhuan Peng was avoiding me everywhere after this incident occurred, and the reason and effect of not replying to my letters.

In his confession, Zhuan Peng listed eleven of his novels. Of course, I don't need to hide it anymore, but for the sake of the truth, I can't let him say it so vaguely. Now I will describe them one by one:

(1) Toothache | It was made by him for Mr. Wang Yixin, because at that time Mr. Wang wanted to start a publication. This manuscript was originally more than 2,000 words long. I added and deleted it twice, increasing it to more than 7,000 words. After Xu Zhimo pointed out some problems, I revised it again, and as a result, only about 6,000 words remained. When revising this article, I used the scenery of Wusong as the background. For example, the evening scene written in the first paragraph is completely my own experience.

(2) A Soldier's Wife | Originally more than 4,000 words long, I increased it to more than 9,000 words. Before revising this article, I had obtained Zhuan Peng's consent. After the Literary Monthly accepted this manuscript, he also knew. At that time, we lived in Shanzhong Road. Zhuan Peng should still remember that it was Mr. Qian Gongxia who lived with us. I think he can also prove it.

(3) The Sixth Birth | As far as I know, the original names are two, one is Cold Night and the other is Life and Death. Last spring, I submitted Zhuan Peng's original manuscript with my name to Dongfang, but it was immediately returned. The editor's reason was... The article was written too hastily, and publishing it would be harmful to me. After a few months, I revised it and showed it to Mr. Chen Fuxi, asking him what title was best. He suggested using The Sixth Birth, and I agreed, but deleted the word "Time". The manuscript was still sent to Dongfang and published in the book.

(4) Fisherman's Joy | Originally named Fishing Boat, Zhuan Peng originally asked Mr. Mu Shiying to take it to Xiandai, but after a long time, it was finally brought back. At that time, I used the scenery of Wujiang as the background and rewrote it three times, adding more than 5,000 words. I think Zhuan Peng should admit it. This article was once submitted to Dongfang Shenbao Monthly and Free Talk, but was not adopted. Later, after a long time, it was published in New China.

(5) Treadmill | Originally named Three People Pumping Water, Zhuan Peng submitted it to Xinyue himself, but it was not used. Later, I revised it twice and changed it to my name and sent it to Xiandai. This manuscript was typed by a certain lady according to my revised manuscript when it was sent to Xiandai. Please ask Mr. Shi Zhicun to prove this. Zhuan Peng told me that this lady could type and was willing to type for me, and he was the one who asked her for me.

(6) Night in the Valley | Originally three to four thousand words long, I revised it and increased it to more than seven thousand words. It was submitted to Xiaoshuo Yuebao but was not accepted, and was later published in Wenyi Yuekan.

(7) Release from Prison | After Zhuan Peng finished writing it, he put it in my drawer for a long time. He and Mr. Fu Shanggao [a good friend who lived with him] both thought it was an unsatisfactory thing. Although there was no time to notify him when revising it, I wrote to him before publishing it. (To be continued)

Miscellaneous Notes on the Journey West (2) 301

— Lu Yan

The passengers on the train were quite crowded. The reason was that the long benches, which could seat three people in a row, were all occupied by those who came first, lying down alone. Therefore, the short benches, which could seat two people in a row, were crowded with people. It was already the second half of the night, and everyone was very tired, leaning their heads against the hard and straight back of the chair, dozing off, sometimes falling down, sometimes tilting left and right, opening their eyes blankly, and closing them drowsily again. This suffering is far greater than that of those who cannot doze off. Most people in the carriage are like this now, and only a few people are sleeping comfortably. This, to a foreigner who doesn't understand the temperament of the Chinese people, I think, he should feel unfair for these many people, or feel the beauty of our Chinese people's humility, right? However, to us, it is not surprising. Now the people squeezed on the short benches, if they had arrived first and saw the long benches empty, would also routinely lie down alone without being polite.

There is only one exception, and that is those hateful waiters. They are waiters, who are supposed to serve the guests, but now they actually occupy two long benches and two short benches. I saw many guests casting angry glances at the two lying waiters.

[Can you let me sleep for a while?] A young man walked over and said very politely.

[Um, um! ...] He replied vaguely. [Talk about it later! I haven't slept for several nights!]

[This guy!] A Western-dressed guest with an eight-character mustache became angry. [This is outrageous! Who gave you the berth? I'll go ask the director later!]

The waiter suddenly woke up, immediately stood up, rubbing his eyes.

[I was really confused in my sleep! Were you the gentleman who wanted a berth just now? ... Okay, okay!] He walked away carrying the bedding.

[Hum! ...] The guest smiled smugly, and went to lie down on the chair, quickly starting to snore sweetly.]

I finally dozed off tiredly for a while.

The older generation got off at Nanjing. I lost a companion. Rong doesn't like to talk, this long journey will be terribly lonely. Unintentionally singing the [Little White Rabbit] that Enge often sang, I thought of Enge and his family, and instead felt more depressed.

That great ferry is just ahead, and I long to see it. I don't know what it looks like, I just vaguely remember that the recent president of a certain college mentioned that ferry in a report on production equipment, so its greatness can be imagined. However, I don't know why, the train just stopped on the river bank between the railway station.

A snack vendor suddenly started asking about his bowls and spoons. He had just brought the food onto the train, delivered it to the guests, and got off the train. Now he came up again, and the guests said someone had taken it. Who? The guests were not clear either. It seemed to be a person wearing black clothes and a felt hat, he said. Many waiters were all looking for and questioning him. They thought that only the Yangzhou waiter's appearance was similar to what the guests said. But he denied ever taking the bowl.

[How many pennies can he earn in a day! To take his bowl!] A strong northern waiter said angrily, walking and searching in the carriage.

A quarter of an hour later, he finally found it. It turned out to be hidden behind the luggage rack at the end of the carriage.

[If it wasn't you, who was it! You were standing at this end!] He said sternly.

The Yangzhou man no longer denied it, just silently lowered his head.

[Village Life in the Boudoir] 302

— Hu Fang

Testament (Two) 303

— Lin Huiyin

["We'll wait here," said Zi Jiu. "I think we should sit together! You don't mind sitting together?"]

While Yina was shaking her head with a smile, Huiqun had already appeared outside the glass door.

["Okay, Miss Song is here!" Zi Jiu cheered.

["You said you were alone," Huiqun said to Yina as she came in, while looking at Song Chen and Zi Jiu.

["You're so late, instead of apologizing, you question people first? And isn't it better to have two more people?"]

["But!"]

["Shouldn't deceive you? Alright, child, just be deceived this once," Yina said, taking Huiqun's hand and walking her inside.

["But we're not allowed to dance today," Huiqun said, after settling down.

["As revenge for being deceived?" Yina asked with a smile. "I completely agree," she said, smiling as she looked at Zi Jiu, because she knew he wouldn't agree.

["Good Miss," Zi Jiu said, "don't get angry like that; we didn't make an appointment, we just bumped into each other at the door."

Huiqun glared at Yina.

Yina just smiled.

["I wonder if Zhichu has come," Zi Jiu said; at the same time, he stood up and took a stroll.

["Didn't see him," Zi Jiu said, returning; "Did you see him dancing?"]

["No," Song Chen replied; then he turned to Yina and said, "I heard from Ye Zhichu that you're writing a long novel for the Literary Weekly?"]

["A novella," Yina said.

["How many words? Is it finished yet?"] Zi Jiu asked.

["About forty to fifty thousand words; haven't started yet."]

Mentioning that novel brought up Yina's worries, and since Ye Zhichu wasn't there, there was an unspeakable desolation stirring beneath her laughter.

["I shouldn't have come here," she regretted privately.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking Points

So This Is What Civilized People Are Like 304

— Yuan

European and American countries constantly accuse us Chinese of being barbaric, while boasting of being civilized. While this is enough to serve as a motto for us Chinese to be vigilant and strive for self-improvement, what we see of so-called civilized people here in Shanghai doesn't necessarily qualify as civilized. If you don't believe me, please look at the news reports about people forcibly taking seats on buses and American women slapping students' faces, only to later claim injury and sue in court, which is just one example.

Giving up seats on streetcars and buses is considered a noble virtue among so-called civilized Europeans and Americans. Every gentleman practices it with humility and courtesy, and it's even more imperative to give up seats to ladies. In the eyes of us Chinese, this is indeed what Confucius meant by [it is unnecessary to dwell on such matters]; however, since the influx of European customs, our Chinese gentlemen of all ages have already [learned and practiced it, which is delightful] on streetcars and buses. Unexpectedly, [learning and practicing it] requires [Chinese learning as the foundation, Western learning for practical application], and incorporating our Chinese national concepts. Therefore, the civilized Europeans and Americans don't quite approve of it. The reason they don't approve, of course, is [you Chinese are a barbaric and lowly race, meant to be servants of Europeans and Americans, so you should give up your seats to civilized Europeans and Americans, and you shouldn't even be allowed to sit with you Chinese. As for us civilized Europeans and Americans giving up our seats to you Chinese, don't even dream about it.] But that day, a certain Chinese student insisted on standing up straight and trying to reason with them, which was naturally his own fault and deserved the lawsuit.

Europeans and Americans boast of being civilized, and our Chinese elites often compare their fellow countrymen to the civilization of Europeans and Americans. However, based on the records in this news report, we should further recognize that the civilization of Europeans and Americans is for Europeans and Americans themselves. We Chinese are not entitled to civilized treatment and should receive the same inferior treatment as the natives of the Americas and Africa.

The court has already accepted the case, and I suppose we'll find out what happens next in the next installment; let's wait and see.

Reflections on the Restoration of the Oriental Library 305

— Liao Zhi

Modern civilization is said to have reached its peak, but what it shows us everywhere is not very [civilized]. To put it bluntly, it is simply the most barbaric of barbarism. Take the January 28th Incident in Shanghai as an example. What the enemy wanted was nothing more than rights and land. They only needed to aim and fire their guns at targets that could hinder them from achieving their goals. Why did they have to bomb our Oriental Library, which had nothing to do with the war, into ashes? Was it a mistake? No, they deliberately wanted to destroy it, because destroying it was tantamount to destroying our culture, or at least inflicting a massive blow on our culture. This heinous act of violence is the civilization presented to us by ambitious imperialists!

The Oriental Library was one of the most significant cultural collections in East Asia. During the January 28th Incident, it was completely destroyed by Japanese artillery fire. This was not only a loss for our country but also a tremendous disaster in the history of world culture!

Our country, which has always prided itself on possessing a four-thousand-year-old culture, may have been a source of glory in the past, but in today's twenty-first century, we see nothing but backwardness in everything. We do not hate the old culture, but we only feel that the times have changed, and the old culture is no longer suitable for present needs. Therefore, if we want to move forward with the times, we should absorb the new culture as much as possible.

The [May Fourth Movement] is said to be the Chinese Renaissance. The new culture at that time showed a vigorous trend. However, due to insufficient material and talent, various cultural undertakings could not be carried out one by one, and the new cultural movement has not yet been fully popularized. In terms of libraries, the most important cultural institutions, there are very few public libraries throughout the country, apart from those attached to major middle schools, and they are all small in scale and poorly equipped. This is still referring to large cities. In small towns, let alone libraries, I'm afraid some don't even have reading rooms! In a country with such a poor cultural infrastructure, it is simply wishful thinking to hope that its culture can be widely disseminated! Fortunately, Shanghai, the cultural hub of the country, established a magnificent and well-equipped Oriental Library in the 13th year of the Republic of China. The people of the country congratulated each other, thinking that our country's old and new cultures would surely be promoted by this, and that the future of culture might receive a ray of light because of this. Who would have thought that it would turn into a scorched earth under the enemy's rain of bullets! Thus, the vast collections of Chinese and foreign books that had been painstakingly collected for thirty years were completely destroyed! In terms of material loss alone, it is at least over a million gold. The huge wound the enemy has inflicted on us truly makes us unable to forget it even in our sleep!

Fortunately, I heard that cultural circles at home and abroad, in view of the destruction of the library, which has had a great and profound impact on social culture and academics, are actively carrying out its restoration, organizing the Oriental Library Restoration Committee, and establishing support committees in Germany, the United States, Britain, and France. It has also established fundraising agencies in seven major cultural centers such as Peiping and Nanking, and hired well-known domestic scholars and international academics as members, with the aim of restoring the old appearance. What a gratifying piece of news! Our restoration of the Oriental Library is not just to seek a new light for China's cultural undertakings; we still have a more significant meaning, that is, on the one hand, to prevent the enemy from ridiculing our country for being unable to recover from a setback; on the other hand, to imply that our nation still has a bit of perseverance and has not given up hope of recovering lost land. We deeply hope that those who care about the country's culture will come forward to enthusiastically provide assistance.

Amateur Mailbox

Reasonable Wage Reduction 306

Editor:

Our XX Silk Weaving Factory can be said to be the largest silk weaving factory in China. Recently, our four thousand workers, unable to bear the factory's repeated wage reductions, went on a full strike on March XX, as I'm sure you know!

This strike is purely based on reasonable demands, because the factory's wage reduction this time is too ruthless, simply wanting to immediately murder our four thousand workers and the lives of their parents, wives, and children! This wage reduction by the factory is already the second or third time. Let's not worry about the past. There was already one reduction last August; after only three or four months, now they announce that wages will be reduced to 70% again. The factory's reason for reducing wages is that the silk market sales are stagnant and the wage burden is too heavy. They call the original wage, which maintained the workers' lives, an unreasonable wage, and further reducing it is considered reasonable. Sir, you can understand that such deceptive words are understood from the facts. First, the factory says sales are down, but according to the manager's announcement to the workers, the total turnover in 1933 was more than 6,020,000 yuan, which has exceeded the records of previous years. Is this really a stagnation in sales! Moreover, in previous years, only two branches specializing in plain fabric weaving had night shifts, but now even the branches weaving patterned fabric also have night shifts. Also, according to a factory employee, soon, all of the XX factories will have to add night shifts. If sales are stagnant, the factory should reduce production. Why would they continue to increase production like this? As for wages, according to the company's announcement, out of the total turnover of 6,020,000 yuan in 1933, the expenditure on salaries and wages was 1,050,000 yuan, accounting for 18% of the total turnover. But in reality, the workers don't get that much; even assuming that the 1,050,000 yuan is entirely the workers' wages, the average annual income of the four thousand workers is only 260 yuan, equivalent to 20 yuan per month. In Shanghai, where the cost of living is very high, can this be considered a lot? Moreover, out of this 1,050,000 yuan, the salaries of the staff, ranging from tens to two or three hundred yuan per month, must also be deducted. So how much do the workers actually get! Also, as the workers' skills improve and output increases greatly, their wages should be slightly increased. This is reasonable for the workers; moreover, the increased production due to the workers' improved skills is beneficial to the factory. Now, they are actually reducing wages because of this, which is truly unreasonable.

Page 22

Furthermore, as machinery becomes increasingly complex, the workers' weaving becomes increasingly difficult. For example, with Hua Silk Georgette, it used to be eighty picks per inch, but now it has to be increased to ninety-six picks per inch; it used to be a single shuttle box, but now they use double shuttle boxes and four shuttle boxes; they used to use single shafts, but now they use double shafts and triple shafts. As such, it is now three or four times more difficult for workers to manage the machinery than before. Workers who used to be able to weave one piece a day can now weave less than one piece, and their wages are less than before. But the factory can increase the selling price because the current products are of better quality, and the wages remain the same, which is actually more profitable than before. Thus, the original wage standard is already an extremely unreasonable standard for the workers. However, the factory is ruthless and not only doesn't increase the original wage but also wants to eliminate it. Isn't this taking the workers' lives! In addition, if workers accidentally damage anything 丨丨 broken ends, oil stains, small flaws, they have to pay compensation; during the renovation period, they are laid off for half a month or a month, and the workers get no wages. As such, the wages workers receive are actually extremely unreasonable.

We will announce other detailed situations in our factory and the suffering of the workers later. In short, in order to live, we work hard every day and exchange our blood and sweat for wages, but according to the newly revised wage standard, our workers really have no way to maintain their lives, so we have to strike and demand that the factory cancel the unreasonable new wage standard.

Right and wrong, truth, will have a public opinion in society. We hope that people from all walks of life and the working masses will give us righteous support!

Sincerely!

XX Factory worker Yao Yunxian, March 14th

The tenth day after the strike

Editor's note: Labor disputes are a major social problem since the development of capitalism. Since then, various people have expressed their solutions from their own perspectives, but although there are many discussions and many solutions, this problem has not yet been resolved, and the disputes are increasingly expanding. Therefore, the editor is unwilling to say more about this problem, fearing that it will only increase theoretical disputes and will not help the actual situation. However, although this problem is large, it is not an unsolvable problem. Although the causes of this problem are extremely complex and related to the social system, it is not without traces. Therefore, although the editor is unwilling to express personal opinions on this issue, based on objective facts, 丨丨 refers to Yao Jun's letter, exploring the characteristics of labor disputes at this stage, although it will not help the efforts of the working masses, it seems to be no more than superfluous words, or it can provide the information to those who care about the problem and are prepared to solve it.

The cause of this strike in Yao Jun's factory was the factory's unwarranted wage reduction. According to Yao Jun, the wage reduction was definitely not due to stagnant sales, and the total turnover was cited as proof. This is certainly true, but it is not known that the factory's move also has its own objective environment. In recent years, the bankruptcy of rural areas and the narrow market for industrial products are known to everyone. The dumping of foreign goods and the difficulty of competition in national industries are known to everyone. The sluggishness of finance and the concentration of investment in public bonds are also known to everyone. Generally speaking, the decline of national industries and the implementation of austerity policies are inevitable results, not the factory's too ruthless heart. The fact that Yao Jun's factory is developing is a fact, but it is also a temporary fortune, a special exception. Although it is difficult to predict its future, it can be said that it cannot always be so smooth and continue to develop. In view of the general economic depression and the uncertainty of the future of business, the factory took this opportunity to try to reduce costs in order to take risks and make a fortune in one fell swoop, which is also human nature. If the market conditions improve in the future, it can continue to move forward according to the normal rules, even if the economic crisis deepens, it will not compensate too much. Therefore, the factory's wage reduction this time was not without reason.

Furthermore, from the perspective of the competition in the employment field, the factory is more likely to reduce wages. The economic situation in the cities has indeed declined significantly, and the number of unemployed people is increasing every day. At the same time, due to the bankruptcy of rural areas, farmers in the interior are leaving their homes and gathering in cities to seek employment. Therefore, the factory has the confidence to reduce wages. The reason why the factory could not reduce wages in the past, or even increase them, was definitely not for the sake of the difficult life of the working masses, and it was not out of pity. The reason for this is that economic development reduces the number of unemployed people and increases the number of workers needed. If the workers unite and strike, it is difficult to recruit so many people to replace them at one time. Now it is different. The workers can strike, but the factory can recruit the same number of people in a matter of days, whether they are skilled or unskilled, which is a matter of raising their hands.

In short, the generation of labor disputes is not due to the labor's unreasonable troubles, nor is it due to the capital's excessive ruthlessness. They are all due to the impossible situation and are controlled by the social environment. Therefore, the disputes in labor issues are actually a reflection of the defects of the entire social system. The resolution of this type of problem is the resolution of social problems, which is also clearly obvious.

[Killing the Family by the Fishing Boat] 307

— Meng

This depicts a story of the oppression of ordinary people in the early imperial era. At that time, there were many common people in Huzhou, Zhejiang, who made a living by fishing. The Xiao En and his daughter Guiying, who are depicted in this picture fishing in the wind and waves, are part of those fishermen. Xiao En and his daughter fish in the wind and waves all day long, and they feel very tired when they go home. Because the wind and waves have been very strong for several days, they get very little fish, and they have run out of rice at home; they feel even more depressed. Guiying knows that her father has sweated a lot and must be very thirsty, so she brings him a cup of tea.

Supplement Editorial Office

Novel

Rain (Three) 309

— Zhang Yiping

Because of the appearance of this person Li Jian, my cousin left without saying goodbye. By the time I knew the news of their secret marriage, they had already gone to Nanjing for their honeymoon. I also rushed to Nanjing like a neurotic, but in the end I couldn't find their traces. (Thinking about it now, if I had found them at the time, what would I have done!) Just then, Zhilin appeared in front of me. She was a classmate of Sister Wen, and we met through Sister Wen's introduction. Speaking of it, I got rid of a Yuan Wen and gained a Zhilin without any effort. In any case, it was worth doing. Moreover, many of my friends were urging the realization of this matter from the side. Naturally, they were all well-intentioned. As for Zhilin, she wasn't necessarily a woman who couldn't inspire love. [Since the other party in our men's love is a woman, Yuan Wen is a woman, and Zhilin is also a woman, can't you love Zhilin just because you're in love with Yuan Wen?] I was once questioned by a friend, but I couldn't say a reason. I regarded such a lovely woman as Zhilin as if I didn't see her. And I listened to my good friend's explanation: [You love Yuan Wen, and Yuan Wen leaves you, and you feel the pain of being lovelorn; similarly, Zhilin loves you, and you don't accept her love, and she feels the same pain of being lovelorn. You should think of others when you think of yourself, and you should combine in every way.]

This again has to say that I am a person who is good at creating troubles for myself. I didn't accept their advice, and I declared that whoever mentioned Yuan Wen and Zhilin again, I would break off friendship with them. Of course, these were angry words; however, it was a fact that I didn't want to hear their names again.

Now, Yuan Wen and I met in a chance place. The man she would rather give up a man who loved her and marry is married to another woman. We were both silent, watching the smoke rings in front of each of us rise up and gradually turn into nothing. The sound of rain outside the window beat on the glass like music, without stopping.

[Yingdi, why don't you talk!] My cousin forced a smile. [Do you think it's an amazing story?]

I shook my head with a smile. [Not really. There are many stories like this!]

Only then did she really smile, and she understood what I meant. [Okay, Yingdi, let's not talk about the past.] Saying this, she picked up a cigarette from the cigarette case.

[Your smoking skills are amazing! Did you learn them recently?]

[Not really, just puffing when I have nothing to do.] She leisurely smoked again. 0

[I'm the same. Sometimes a can of cigarettes sits there for a whole week, and sometimes it's finished in one or two days.]

Like __________ talking to her about these irrelevant topics, I seemed to want to laugh. How clever humans are, easily敷衍ing over a serious situation. My cousin seemed to understand that although she was telling me the story as if it were a joke, it was somewhat reluctant. Smoking, forced laughter, were all trying to dilute the image of this question. The two exchanged glances, and then there was a sudden silence.
